21
22bool DecodeLocalDecls(const WasmFeatures& enabled, BodyLocalDecls* decls,
23 const byte* start, const byte* end) {
24 WasmFeatures no_features = WasmFeatures::None();
25 Zone* zone = decls->type_list.get_allocator().zone();
26 WasmDecoder<Decoder::kValidate> decoder(zone, nullptr, enabled, &no_features,
27 nullptr, start, end, 0);
28 uint32_t length;
29 if (!decoder.DecodeLocals(decoder.pc(), &length, 0)) {
30 decls->encoded_size = 0;
31 return false;
32 }
33 DCHECK(decoder.ok())((void) 0);
34 decls->encoded_size = length;
35 // Copy the decoded locals types into {decls->type_list}.
36 DCHECK(decls->type_list.empty())((void) 0);
37 decls->type_list = std::move(decoder.local_types_);
38 return true;
39}
40
41BytecodeIterator::BytecodeIterator(const byte* start, const byte* end,
42 BodyLocalDecls* decls)
43 : Decoder(start, end) {
44 if (decls != nullptr) {
45 if (DecodeLocalDecls(WasmFeatures::All(), decls, start, end)) {
46 pc_ += decls->encoded_size;
47 if (pc_ > end_) pc_ = end_;
48 }
49 }
50}
51
52DecodeResult VerifyWasmCode(AccountingAllocator* allocator,
53 const WasmFeatures& enabled,
54 const WasmModule* module, WasmFeatures* detected,
55 const FunctionBody& body) {
56 Zone zone(allocator, ZONE_NAME__func__);
57 WasmFullDecoder<Decoder::kValidate, EmptyInterface> decoder(
58 &zone, module, enabled, detected, body);
59 decoder.Decode();
60 return decoder.toResult(nullptr);
61}
62
63unsigned OpcodeLength(const byte* pc, const byte* end) {
64 WasmFeatures no_features = WasmFeatures::None();
65 Zone* no_zone = nullptr;
66 WasmModule* no_module = nullptr;
67 FunctionSig* no_sig = nullptr;
68 WasmDecoder<Decoder::kNoValidate> decoder(no_zone, no_module, no_features,
69 &no_features, no_sig, pc, end, 0);
70 return WasmDecoder<Decoder::kNoValidate>::OpcodeLength(&decoder, pc);
71}
72
73std::pair<uint32_t, uint32_t> StackEffect(const WasmModule* module,
74 const FunctionSig* sig,
75 const byte* pc, const byte* end) {
76 WasmFeatures unused_detected_features = WasmFeatures::None();
77 Zone* no_zone = nullptr;
78 WasmDecoder<Decoder::kNoValidate> decoder(
79 no_zone, module, WasmFeatures::All(), &unused_detected_features, sig, pc,
80 end);
81 return decoder.StackEffect(pc);
82}

103const char* PrefixName(WasmOpcode prefix_opcode) {
104 switch (prefix_opcode) {
105#define DECLARE_PREFIX_CASE(name, opcode) \
106 case k##name##Prefix: \
107 return "k" #name "Prefix";

130V8_INLINEinline __attribute__((always_inline)) WasmFeature feature_for_heap_type(HeapType heap_type) {
131 switch (heap_type.representation()) {
132 case HeapType::kFunc:
133 case HeapType::kExtern:
134 return WasmFeature::kFeature_reftypes;
135 case HeapType::kExn:
136 return WasmFeature::kFeature_eh;
137 case HeapType::kEq:
138 case HeapType::kI31:
139 return WasmFeature::kFeature_gc;
140 default:
141 UNREACHABLE()V8_Fatal("unreachable code");
142 }
143}
144
145template <Decoder::ValidateFlag validate>
146HeapType read_heap_type(Decoder* decoder, const byte* pc,
147 uint32_t* const length, const WasmFeatures& enabled) {
148 int64_t heap_index = decoder->read_i33v<validate>(pc, length, "heap type");
149 if (heap_index < 0) {
150 uint8_t uint_7_mask = 0x7F;
151 uint8_t code = static_cast<ValueTypeCode>(heap_index) & uint_7_mask;
152 switch (code) {
153 case kLocalFuncRef:
154 case kLocalExnRef:
155 case kLocalEqRef:
156 case kLocalExternRef:
157 case kLocalI31Ref: {
158 HeapType result = HeapType::from_code(code);
159 if (!VALIDATE(enabled.contains(feature_for_heap_type(result)))) {
160 decoder->errorf(
161 pc, "invalid heap type '%s', enable with --experimental-wasm-%s",
162 result.name().c_str(),
163 WasmFeatures::name_for_feature(feature_for_heap_type(result)));
164 return HeapType(HeapType::kBottom);
165 }
166 return result;
167 }
168 default:
169 if (validate) {
170 decoder->errorf(pc, "Unknown heap type %" PRId64"l" "d", heap_index);
171 }
172 return HeapType(HeapType::kBottom);
173 }
174 UNREACHABLE()V8_Fatal("unreachable code");
175 } else {
176 if (!VALIDATE(enabled.has_typed_funcref())) {
177 decoder->error(pc,
178 "Invalid indexed heap type, enable with "
179 "--experimental-wasm-typed-funcref");
180 return HeapType(HeapType::kBottom);
181 }
182 uint32_t type_index = static_cast<uint32_t>(heap_index);
183 if (!VALIDATE(type_index < kV8MaxWasmTypes)) {
184 decoder->errorf(pc,
185 "Type index %u is greater than the maximum number %zu "
186 "of type definitions supported by V8",
187 type_index, kV8MaxWasmTypes);
188 return HeapType(HeapType::kBottom);
189 }
190 return HeapType(type_index);
191 }
192}
193
194// Read a value type starting at address 'pc' in 'decoder'.
195// No bytes are consumed. The result is written into the 'result' parameter.
196// Returns the amount of bytes read, or 0 if decoding failed.
197// Registers an error if the type opcode is invalid iff validate is set.
198template <Decoder::ValidateFlag validate>
199ValueType read_value_type(Decoder* decoder, const byte* pc,
200 uint32_t* const length, const WasmFeatures& enabled) {
201 *length = 1;
202 byte val = decoder->read_u8<validate>(pc, "value type opcode");
203 if (decoder->failed()) {
204 return kWasmBottom;
205 }
206 ValueTypeCode code = static_cast<ValueTypeCode>(val);
207 switch (code) {
208 case kLocalFuncRef:
209 case kLocalExnRef:
210 case kLocalEqRef:
211 case kLocalExternRef:
212 case kLocalI31Ref: {
213 HeapType heap_type = HeapType::from_code(code);
214 ValueType result = ValueType::Ref(heap_type, kNullable);
215 if (!VALIDATE(enabled.contains(feature_for_heap_type(heap_type)))) {
216 decoder->errorf(
217 pc, "invalid value type '%s', enable with --experimental-wasm-%s",
218 result.name().c_str(),
219 WasmFeatures::name_for_feature(feature_for_heap_type(heap_type)));
220 return kWasmBottom;
221 }
222 return result;
223 }
224 case kLocalI32:
225 return kWasmI32;
226 case kLocalI64:
227 return kWasmI64;
228 case kLocalF32:
229 return kWasmF32;
230 case kLocalF64:
231 return kWasmF64;
232 case kLocalRef:
233 case kLocalOptRef: {
234 Nullability nullability = code == kLocalOptRef ? kNullable : kNonNullable;
235 if (!VALIDATE(enabled.has_typed_funcref())) {
236 decoder->errorf(pc,
237 "Invalid type 'ref%s', enable with "
238 "--experimental-wasm-typed-funcref",
239 nullability == kNullable ? " null" : "");
240 return kWasmBottom;
241 }
242 HeapType heap_type =
243 read_heap_type<validate>(decoder, pc + 1, length, enabled);
244 *length += 1;
245 return heap_type.is_bottom() ? kWasmBottom
246 : ValueType::Ref(heap_type, nullability);
247 }
248 case kLocalRtt: {
249 if (!VALIDATE(enabled.has_gc())) {
250 decoder->error(
251 pc, "invalid value type 'rtt', enable with --experimental-wasm-gc");
252 return kWasmBottom;
253 }
254 uint32_t depth_length;
255 uint32_t depth =
256 decoder->read_u32v<validate>(pc + 1, &depth_length, "depth");
257 // TODO(7748): Introduce a proper limit.
258 const uint32_t kMaxRttSubtypingDepth = 7;
259 if (!VALIDATE(depth <= kMaxRttSubtypingDepth)) {
260 decoder->errorf(pc,
261 "subtyping depth %u is greater than the maximum depth "
262 "%u supported by V8",
263 depth, kMaxRttSubtypingDepth);
264 return kWasmBottom;
265 }
266 HeapType heap_type = read_heap_type<validate>(
267 decoder, pc + depth_length + 1, length, enabled);
268 *length += depth_length + 1;
269 return heap_type.is_bottom() ? kWasmBottom
270 : ValueType::Rtt(heap_type, depth);
271 }
272 case kLocalS128:
273 if (!VALIDATE(enabled.has_simd())) {
274 decoder->error(pc,
275 "invalid value type 'Simd128', enable with "
276 "--experimental-wasm-simd");
277 return kWasmBottom;
278 }
279 return kWasmS128;
280 case kLocalVoid:
281 case kLocalI8:
282 case kLocalI16:
283 // Although these types are included in ValueType, they are technically
284 // not value types and are only used in specific contexts. The caller of
285 // this function is responsible to check for them separately.
286 break;
287 }
288 // Malformed modules specifying invalid types can get here.
289 return kWasmBottom;
290}
291} // namespace value_type_reader
292
293// Helpers for decoding different kinds of immediates which follow bytecodes.
294template <Decoder::ValidateFlag validate>
295struct LocalIndexImmediate {
296 uint32_t index;

333template <Decoder::ValidateFlag validate>
334struct ImmF32Immediate {
335 float value;
336 uint32_t length = 4;
337 inline ImmF32Immediate(Decoder* decoder, const byte* pc) {
338 // We can't use bit_cast here because calling any helper function that
339 // returns a float would potentially flip NaN bits per C++ semantics, so we
340 // have to inline the memcpy call directly.
341 uint32_t tmp = decoder->read_u32<validate>(pc, "immf32");
342 memcpy(&value, &tmp, sizeof(value));
343 }
344};
345
346template <Decoder::ValidateFlag validate>
347struct ImmF64Immediate {
348 double value;
349 uint32_t length = 8;
350 inline ImmF64Immediate(Decoder* decoder, const byte* pc) {
351 // Avoid bit_cast because it might not preserve the signalling bit of a NaN.
352 uint64_t tmp = decoder->read_u64<validate>(pc, "immf64");
353 memcpy(&value, &tmp, sizeof(value));
354 }
355};

369template <Decoder::ValidateFlag validate>
370struct SelectTypeImmediate {
371 uint32_t length;
372 ValueType type;
373
374 inline SelectTypeImmediate(const WasmFeatures& enabled, Decoder* decoder,
375 const byte* pc) {
376 uint8_t num_types =
377 decoder->read_u32v<validate>(pc, &length, "number of select types");
378 if (!VALIDATE(num_types == 1)) {
379 decoder->error(
380 pc + 1, "Invalid number of types. Select accepts exactly one type");
381 return;
382 }
383 uint32_t type_length;
384 type = value_type_reader::read_value_type<validate>(decoder, pc + length,
385 &type_length, enabled);
386 length += type_length;
387 if (!VALIDATE(type != kWasmBottom)) {
388 decoder->error(pc + 1, "invalid select type");
389 }
390 }
391};

533template <Decoder::ValidateFlag validate>
534struct CallIndirectImmediate {
535 uint32_t table_index;
536 uint32_t sig_index;
537 const FunctionSig* sig = nullptr;
538 uint32_t length = 0;
539 inline CallIndirectImmediate(const WasmFeatures enabled, Decoder* decoder,
540 const byte* pc) {
541 uint32_t len = 0;
542 sig_index = decoder->read_u32v<validate>(pc, &len, "signature index");
543 TableIndexImmediate<validate> table(decoder, pc + len);
544 if (!VALIDATE((table.index == 0 && table.length == 1) ||
545 enabled.has_reftypes())) {
546 decoder->errorf(pc + len, "expected table index 0, found %u",
547 table.index);
548 }
549 table_index = table.index;
550 length = len + table.length;
551 }
552};

564template <Decoder::ValidateFlag validate>
565struct BranchTableImmediate {
566 uint32_t table_count;
567 const byte* start;
568 const byte* table;
569 inline BranchTableImmediate(Decoder* decoder, const byte* pc) {
570 start = pc;
571 uint32_t len = 0;
572 table_count = decoder->read_u32v<validate>(pc, &len, "table count");
573 table = pc + len;
574 }
575};
576
577// A helper to iterate over a branch table.
578template <Decoder::ValidateFlag validate>
579class BranchTableIterator {
580 public:
581 uint32_t cur_index() { return index_; }
582 bool has_next() { return VALIDATE(decoder_->ok()) && index_ <= table_count_; }
583 uint32_t next() {
584 DCHECK(has_next())((void) 0);
585 index_++;
586 uint32_t length;
587 uint32_t result =
588 decoder_->read_u32v<validate>(pc_, &length, "branch table entry");
589 pc_ += length;
590 return result;
591 }
592 // length, including the length of the {BranchTableImmediate}, but not the
593 // opcode.
594 uint32_t length() {
595 while (has_next()) next();
596 return static_cast<uint32_t>(pc_ - start_);
597 }
598 const byte* pc() { return pc_; }
599
600 BranchTableIterator(Decoder* decoder,
601 const BranchTableImmediate<validate>& imm)
602 : decoder_(decoder),
603 start_(imm.start),
604 pc_(imm.table),
605 table_count_(imm.table_count) {}
606
607 private:
608 Decoder* const decoder_;
609 const byte* start_;
610 const byte* pc_;
611 uint32_t index_ = 0; // the current index.
612 const uint32_t table_count_; // the count of entries, not including default.
613};
614
615template <Decoder::ValidateFlag validate>
616struct MemoryAccessImmediate {
617 uint32_t alignment;
618 uint32_t offset;
619 uint32_t length = 0;
620 inline MemoryAccessImmediate(Decoder* decoder, const byte* pc,
621 uint32_t max_alignment) {
622 uint32_t alignment_length;
623 alignment =
624 decoder->read_u32v<validate>(pc, &alignment_length, "alignment");
625 if (!VALIDATE(alignment <= max_alignment)) {
626 decoder->errorf(pc,
627 "invalid alignment; expected maximum alignment is %u, "
628 "actual alignment is %u",
629 max_alignment, alignment);
630 }
631 uint32_t offset_length;
632 offset = decoder->read_u32v<validate>(pc + alignment_length, &offset_length,
633 "offset");
634 length = alignment_length + offset_length;
635 }
636};

749// An entry on the value stack.
750struct ValueBase {
751 const byte* pc = nullptr;
752 ValueType type = kWasmStmt;
753
754 ValueBase(const byte* pc, ValueType type) : pc(pc), type(type) {}
755};
756
757template <typename Value>
758struct Merge {
759 uint32_t arity = 0;
760 union { // Either multiple values or a single value.
761 Value* array;
762 Value first;
763 } vals = {nullptr}; // Initialize {array} with {nullptr}.
764
765 // Tracks whether this merge was ever reached. Uses precise reachability, like
766 // Reachability::kReachable.
767 bool reached;
768
769 explicit Merge(bool reached = false) : reached(reached) {}
770
771 Value& operator[](uint32_t i) {
772 DCHECK_GT(arity, i)((void) 0);
773 return arity == 1 ? vals.first : vals.array[i];
774 }
775};
776
777enum ControlKind : uint8_t {
778 kControlIf,
779 kControlIfElse,
780 kControlBlock,
781 kControlLoop,
782 kControlLet,
783 kControlTry,
784 kControlTryCatch
785};
786
787enum Reachability : uint8_t {
788 // reachable code.
789 kReachable,
790 // reachable code in unreachable block (implies normal validation).
791 kSpecOnlyReachable,
792 // code unreachable in its own block (implies polymorphic validation).
793 kUnreachable
794};
795
796// An entry on the control stack (i.e. if, block, loop, or try).
797template <typename Value>
798struct ControlBase {
799 ControlKind kind = kControlBlock;
800 uint32_t locals_count = 0;
801 uint32_t stack_depth = 0; // stack height at the beginning of the construct.
802 const uint8_t* pc = nullptr;
803 Reachability reachability = kReachable;
804
805 // Values merged into the start or end of this control construct.
806 Merge<Value> start_merge;
807 Merge<Value> end_merge;
808
809 MOVE_ONLY_NO_DEFAULT_CONSTRUCTOR(ControlBase)ControlBase(ControlBase&&) noexcept = default; ControlBase
& operator=(ControlBase&&) noexcept = default; ControlBase
(const ControlBase&) = delete; ControlBase& operator=
(const ControlBase&) = delete;
810
811 ControlBase(ControlKind kind, uint32_t locals_count, uint32_t stack_depth,
812 const uint8_t* pc, Reachability reachability)
813 : kind(kind),
814 locals_count(locals_count),
815 stack_depth(stack_depth),
816 pc(pc),
817 reachability(reachability),
818 start_merge(reachability == kReachable) {
819 DCHECK(kind == kControlLet || locals_count == 0)((void) 0);
820 }
821
822 // Check whether the current block is reachable.
823 bool reachable() const { return reachability == kReachable; }
824
825 // Check whether the rest of the block is unreachable.
826 // Note that this is different from {!reachable()}, as there is also the
827 // "indirect unreachable state", for which both {reachable()} and
828 // {unreachable()} return false.
829 bool unreachable() const { return reachability == kUnreachable; }
830
831 // Return the reachability of new control structs started in this block.
832 Reachability innerReachability() const {
833 return reachability == kReachable ? kReachable : kSpecOnlyReachable;
834 }
835
836 bool is_if() const { return is_onearmed_if() || is_if_else(); }
837 bool is_onearmed_if() const { return kind == kControlIf; }
838 bool is_if_else() const { return kind == kControlIfElse; }
839 bool is_block() const { return kind == kControlBlock; }
840 bool is_let() const { return kind == kControlLet; }
841 bool is_loop() const { return kind == kControlLoop; }
842 bool is_incomplete_try() const { return kind == kControlTry; }
843 bool is_try_catch() const { return kind == kControlTryCatch; }
844 bool is_try() const { return is_incomplete_try() || is_try_catch(); }
845
846 inline Merge<Value>* br_merge() {
847 return is_loop() ? &this->start_merge : &this->end_merge;
848 }
849};

987// Generic Wasm bytecode decoder with utilities for decoding immediates,
988// lengths, etc.
989template <Decoder::ValidateFlag validate>
990class WasmDecoder : public Decoder {
991 public:
992 WasmDecoder(Zone* zone, const WasmModule* module, const WasmFeatures& enabled,
993 WasmFeatures* detected, const FunctionSig* sig, const byte* start,
994 const byte* end, uint32_t buffer_offset = 0)
995 : Decoder(start, end, buffer_offset),
996 local_types_(zone),
997 module_(module),
998 enabled_(enabled),
999 detected_(detected),
1000 sig_(sig) {}
1001
1002 Zone* zone() const { return local_types_.get_allocator().zone(); }
1003
1004 uint32_t num_locals() const {
1005 return static_cast<uint32_t>(local_types_.size());
1006 }
1007
1008 ValueType local_type(uint32_t index) const { return local_types_[index]; }
1009
1010 void InitializeLocalsFromSig() {
1011 DCHECK_NOT_NULL(sig_)((void) 0);
1012 DCHECK_EQ(0, this->local_types_.size())((void) 0);
1013 local_types_.assign(sig_->parameters().begin(), sig_->parameters().end());
1014 }
1015
1016 // Decodes local definitions in the current decoder.
1017 // Returns true iff locals are found.
1018 // Writes the total length of decoded locals in 'total_length'.
1019 // If insert_postion is present, the decoded locals will be inserted into the
1020 // 'local_types_' of this decoder. Otherwise, this function is used just to
1021 // check validity and determine the encoding length of the locals in bytes.
1022 // The decoder's pc is not advanced. If no locals are found (i.e., no
1023 // compressed uint32 is found at pc), this will exit as 'false' and without an
1024 // error.
1025 bool DecodeLocals(const byte* pc, uint32_t* total_length,
1026 const base::Optional<uint32_t> insert_position) {
1027 uint32_t length;
1028 *total_length = 0;
1029
1030 // The 'else' value is useless, we pass it for convenience.
1031 auto insert_iterator = insert_position.has_value()
1032 ? local_types_.begin() + insert_position.value()
1033 : local_types_.begin();
1034
1035 // Decode local declarations, if any.
1036 uint32_t entries = read_u32v<kValidate>(pc, &length, "local decls count");
1037 if (!VALIDATE(ok())) {
1038 error(pc + *total_length, "invalid local decls count");
1039 return false;
1040 }
1041
1042 *total_length += length;
1043 TRACE("local decls count: %u\n", entries);
1044
1045 while (entries-- > 0) {
1046 if (!VALIDATE(more())) {
1047 error(end(), "expected more local decls but reached end of input");
1048 return false;
1049 }
1050 uint32_t count =
1051 read_u32v<kValidate>(pc + *total_length, &length, "local count");
1052 if (!VALIDATE(ok())) {
1053 error(pc + *total_length, "invalid local count");
1054 return false;
1055 }
1056 DCHECK_LE(local_types_.size(), kV8MaxWasmFunctionLocals)((void) 0);
1057 if (!VALIDATE(count <= kV8MaxWasmFunctionLocals - local_types_.size())) {
1058 error(pc + *total_length, "local count too large");
1059 return false;
1060 }
1061 *total_length += length;
1062
1063 ValueType type = value_type_reader::read_value_type<kValidate>(
1064 this, pc + *total_length, &length, enabled_);
1065 if (!VALIDATE(type != kWasmBottom)) {
1066 error(pc + *total_length, "invalid local type");
1067 return false;
1068 }
1069 *total_length += length;
1070
1071 if (insert_position.has_value()) {
1072 // Move the insertion iterator to the end of the newly inserted locals.
1073 insert_iterator =
1074 local_types_.insert(insert_iterator, count, type) + count;
1075 }
1076 }
1077 DCHECK(ok())((void) 0);
1078 return true;
1079 }
1080
1081 static BitVector* AnalyzeLoopAssignment(WasmDecoder* decoder, const byte* pc,
1082 uint32_t locals_count, Zone* zone) {
1083 if (pc >= decoder->end()) return nullptr;
1084 if (*pc != kExprLoop) return nullptr;
1085
1086 // The number of locals_count is augmented by 2 so that 'locals_count - 2'
1087 // can be used to track mem_size, and 'locals_count - 1' to track mem_start.
1088 BitVector* assigned = zone->New<BitVector>(locals_count, zone);
1089 int depth = 0;
1090 // Iteratively process all AST nodes nested inside the loop.
1091 while (pc < decoder->end() && VALIDATE(decoder->ok())) {
1092 WasmOpcode opcode = static_cast<WasmOpcode>(*pc);
1093 uint32_t length = 1;
1094 switch (opcode) {
1095 case kExprLoop:
1096 case kExprIf:
1097 case kExprBlock:
1098 case kExprTry:
1099 length = OpcodeLength(decoder, pc);
1100 depth++;
1101 break;
1102 case kExprLocalSet: // fallthru
1103 case kExprLocalTee: {
1104 LocalIndexImmediate<validate> imm(decoder, pc + 1);
1105 if (assigned->length() > 0 &&
1106 imm.index < static_cast<uint32_t>(assigned->length())) {
1107 // Unverified code might have an out-of-bounds index.
1108 assigned->Add(imm.index);
1109 }
1110 length = 1 + imm.length;
1111 break;
1112 }
1113 case kExprMemoryGrow:
1114 case kExprCallFunction:
1115 case kExprCallIndirect:
1116 case kExprReturnCall:
1117 case kExprReturnCallIndirect:
1118 // Add instance cache nodes to the assigned set.
1119 // TODO(titzer): make this more clear.
1120 assigned->Add(locals_count - 1);
1121 length = OpcodeLength(decoder, pc);
1122 break;
1123 case kExprEnd:
1124 depth--;
1125 break;
1126 default:
1127 length = OpcodeLength(decoder, pc);
1128 break;
1129 }
1130 if (depth <= 0) break;
1131 pc += length;
1132 }
1133 return VALIDATE(decoder->ok()) ? assigned : nullptr;
1134 }

1136 inline bool Validate(const byte* pc, LocalIndexImmediate<validate>& imm) {
1137 if (!VALIDATE(imm.index < num_locals())) {
1138 errorf(pc, "invalid local index: %u", imm.index);
1139 return false;
1140 }
1141 return true;
1142 }

1144 inline bool Complete(ExceptionIndexImmediate<validate>& imm) {
1145 if (!VALIDATE(imm.index < module_->exceptions.size())) return false;
1146 imm.exception = &module_->exceptions[imm.index];
1147 return true;
1148 }

1150 inline bool Validate(const byte* pc, ExceptionIndexImmediate<validate>& imm) {
1151 if (!Complete(imm)) {
1152 errorf(pc, "Invalid exception index: %u", imm.index);
1153 return false;
1154 }
1155 return true;
1156 }

1158 inline bool Validate(const byte* pc, GlobalIndexImmediate<validate>& imm) {
1159 if (!VALIDATE(imm.index < module_->globals.size())) {
1160 errorf(pc, "invalid global index: %u", imm.index);
1161 return false;
1162 }
1163 imm.global = &module_->globals[imm.index];
1164 imm.type = imm.global->type;
1165 return true;
1166 }

1168 inline bool Complete(StructIndexImmediate<validate>& imm) {
1169 if (!VALIDATE(module_->has_struct(imm.index))) return false;
1170 imm.struct_type = module_->struct_type(imm.index);
1171 return true;
1172 }
1173
1174 inline bool Validate(const byte* pc, StructIndexImmediate<validate>& imm) {
1175 if (Complete(imm)) return true;
1176 errorf(pc, "invalid struct index: %u", imm.index);
1177 return false;
1178 }
1179
1180 inline bool Validate(const byte* pc, FieldIndexImmediate<validate>& imm) {
1181 if (!Validate(pc, imm.struct_index)) return false;
1182 if (!VALIDATE(imm.index < imm.struct_index.struct_type->field_count())) {
1183 errorf(pc + imm.struct_index.length, "invalid field index: %u",
1184 imm.index);
1185 return false;
1186 }
1187 return true;
1188 }

1190 inline bool Complete(ArrayIndexImmediate<validate>& imm) {
1191 if (!VALIDATE(module_->has_array(imm.index))) return false;
1192 imm.array_type = module_->array_type(imm.index);
1193 return true;
1194 }

1196 inline bool Validate(const byte* pc, ArrayIndexImmediate<validate>& imm) {
1197 if (!Complete(imm)) {
1198 errorf(pc, "invalid array index: %u", imm.index);
1199 return false;
1200 }
1201 return true;
1202 }
1203
1204 inline bool CanReturnCall(const FunctionSig* target_sig) {
1205 if (target_sig == nullptr) return false;
1206 size_t num_returns = sig_->return_count();
1207 if (num_returns != target_sig->return_count()) return false;
1208 for (size_t i = 0; i < num_returns; ++i) {
1209 if (sig_->GetReturn(i) != target_sig->GetReturn(i)) return false;
1210 }
1211 return true;
1212 }
1213
1214 inline bool Complete(CallFunctionImmediate<validate>& imm) {
1215 if (!VALIDATE(imm.index < module_->functions.size())) return false;
1216 imm.sig = module_->functions[imm.index].sig;
1217 if (imm.sig->return_count() > 1) {
1218 this->detected_->Add(kFeature_mv);
1219 }
1220 return true;
1221 }
1222
1223 inline bool Validate(const byte* pc, CallFunctionImmediate<validate>& imm) {
1224 if (!Complete(imm)) {
1225 errorf(pc, "invalid function index: %u", imm.index);
1226 return false;
1227 }
1228 return true;
1229 }
1230
1231 inline bool Complete(CallIndirectImmediate<validate>& imm) {
1232 if (!VALIDATE(module_->has_signature(imm.sig_index))) return false;
1233 imm.sig = module_->signature(imm.sig_index);
1234 if (imm.sig->return_count() > 1) {
1235 this->detected_->Add(kFeature_mv);
1236 }
1237 return true;
1238 }
1239
1240 inline bool Validate(const byte* pc, CallIndirectImmediate<validate>& imm) {
1241 if (!VALIDATE(imm.table_index < module_->tables.size())) {
1242 error("function table has to exist to execute call_indirect");
1243 return false;
1244 }
1245 if (!VALIDATE(IsSubtypeOf(module_->tables[imm.table_index].type,
1246 kWasmFuncRef, module_))) {
1247 error("table of call_indirect must be of a function type");
1248 return false;
1249 }
1250 if (!Complete(imm)) {
1251 errorf(pc, "invalid signature index: #%u", imm.sig_index);
1252 return false;
1253 }
1254 // Check that the dynamic signature for this call is a subtype of the static
1255 // type of the table the function is defined in.
1256 if (!VALIDATE(IsSubtypeOf(ValueType::Ref(imm.sig_index, kNonNullable),
1257 module_->tables[imm.table_index].type,
1258 module_))) {
1259 errorf(pc,
1260 "call_indirect: Signature of function %u is not a subtype of "
1261 "table %u",
1262 imm.sig_index, imm.table_index);
1263 }
1264 return true;
1265 }
1266
1267 inline bool Validate(const byte* pc, BranchDepthImmediate<validate>& imm,
1268 size_t control_depth) {
1269 if (!VALIDATE(imm.depth < control_depth)) {
1270 errorf(pc, "invalid branch depth: %u", imm.depth);
1271 return false;
1272 }
1273 return true;
1274 }
1275
1276 inline bool Validate(const byte* pc, BranchTableImmediate<validate>& imm,
1277 size_t block_depth) {
1278 if (!VALIDATE(imm.table_count <= kV8MaxWasmFunctionBrTableSize)) {
1279 errorf(pc, "invalid table count (> max br_table size): %u",
1280 imm.table_count);
1281 return false;
1282 }
1283 return checkAvailable(imm.table_count);
1284 }
1285
1286 inline bool Validate(const byte* pc,
1287 BranchOnExceptionImmediate<validate>& imm,
1288 size_t control_size) {
1289 return Validate(pc, imm.depth, control_size) &&
1290 Validate(pc + imm.depth.length, imm.index);
1291 }
1292
1293 inline bool Validate(const byte* pc, WasmOpcode opcode,
1294 SimdLaneImmediate<validate>& imm) {
1295 uint8_t num_lanes = 0;
1296 switch (opcode) {
1297 case kExprF64x2ExtractLane:
1298 case kExprF64x2ReplaceLane:
1299 case kExprI64x2ExtractLane:
1300 case kExprI64x2ReplaceLane:
1301 num_lanes = 2;
1302 break;
1303 case kExprF32x4ExtractLane:
1304 case kExprF32x4ReplaceLane:
1305 case kExprI32x4ExtractLane:
1306 case kExprI32x4ReplaceLane:
1307 num_lanes = 4;
1308 break;
1309 case kExprI16x8ExtractLaneS:
1310 case kExprI16x8ExtractLaneU:
1311 case kExprI16x8ReplaceLane:
1312 num_lanes = 8;
1313 break;
1314 case kExprI8x16ExtractLaneS:
1315 case kExprI8x16ExtractLaneU:
1316 case kExprI8x16ReplaceLane:
1317 num_lanes = 16;
1318 break;
1319 default:
1320 UNREACHABLE()V8_Fatal("unreachable code");
1321 break;
1322 }
1323 if (!VALIDATE(imm.lane >= 0 && imm.lane < num_lanes)) {
1324 error(pc, "invalid lane index");
1325 return false;
1326 } else {
1327 return true;
1328 }
1329 }
1330
1331 inline bool Validate(const byte* pc, Simd128Immediate<validate>& imm) {
1332 uint8_t max_lane = 0;
1333 for (uint32_t i = 0; i < kSimd128Size; ++i) {
1334 max_lane = std::max(max_lane, imm.value[i]);
1335 }
1336 // Shuffle indices must be in [0..31] for a 16 lane shuffle.
1337 if (!VALIDATE(max_lane < 2 * kSimd128Size)) {
1338 error(pc, "invalid shuffle mask");
1339 return false;
1340 }
1341 return true;
1342 }
1343
1344 inline bool Complete(BlockTypeImmediate<validate>& imm) {
1345 if (imm.type != kWasmBottom) return true;
30
←
Assuming the condition is true
→
31
←
Taking true branch
→
32
←
Returning without writing to 'imm.sig'
→
1346 if (!VALIDATE(module_->has_signature(imm.sig_index))) return false;
1347 imm.sig = module_->signature(imm.sig_index);
1348 if (imm.sig->return_count() > 1) {
1349 this->detected_->Add(kFeature_mv);
1350 }
1351 return true;
1352 }
1353
1354 inline bool Validate(const byte* pc, BlockTypeImmediate<validate>& imm) {
1355 if (!Complete(imm)) {
1356 errorf(pc, "block type index %u out of bounds (%zu types)", imm.sig_index,
1357 module_->types.size());
1358 return false;
1359 }
1360 return true;
1361 }
1362
1363 inline bool Validate(const byte* pc, FunctionIndexImmediate<validate>& imm) {
1364 if (!VALIDATE(imm.index < module_->functions.size())) {
1365 errorf(pc, "invalid function index: %u", imm.index);
1366 return false;
1367 }
1368 if (!VALIDATE(module_->functions[imm.index].declared)) {
1369 this->errorf(pc, "undeclared reference to function #%u", imm.index);
1370 return false;
1371 }
1372 return true;
1373 }

1375 inline bool Validate(const byte* pc, MemoryIndexImmediate<validate>& imm) {
1376 if (!VALIDATE(module_->has_memory)) {
1377 errorf(pc, "memory instruction with no memory");
1378 return false;
1379 }
1380 return true;
1381 }

1383 inline bool Validate(const byte* pc, MemoryInitImmediate<validate>& imm) {
1384 if (!VALIDATE(imm.data_segment_index <
1385 module_->num_declared_data_segments)) {
1386 errorf(pc, "invalid data segment index: %u", imm.data_segment_index);
1387 return false;
1388 }
1389 if (!Validate(pc + imm.length - imm.memory.length, imm.memory))
1390 return false;
1391 return true;
1392 }
1393
1394 inline bool Validate(const byte* pc, DataDropImmediate<validate>& imm) {
1395 if (!VALIDATE(imm.index < module_->num_declared_data_segments)) {
1396 errorf(pc, "invalid data segment index: %u", imm.index);
1397 return false;
1398 }
1399 return true;
1400 }

1402 inline bool Validate(const byte* pc, MemoryCopyImmediate<validate>& imm) {
1403 return Validate(pc, imm.memory_src) &&
1404 Validate(pc + imm.memory_src.length, imm.memory_dst);
1405 }

1407 inline bool Validate(const byte* pc, TableIndexImmediate<validate>& imm) {
1408 if (!VALIDATE(imm.index < module_->tables.size())) {
1409 errorf(pc, "invalid table index: %u", imm.index);
1410 return false;
1411 }
1412 return true;
1413 }
1414
1415 inline bool Validate(const byte* pc, TableInitImmediate<validate>& imm) {
1416 if (!VALIDATE(imm.elem_segment_index < module_->elem_segments.size())) {
1417 errorf(pc, "invalid element segment index: %u", imm.elem_segment_index);
1418 return false;
1419 }
1420 if (!Validate(pc + imm.length - imm.table.length, imm.table)) {
1421 return false;
1422 }
1423 ValueType elem_type = module_->elem_segments[imm.elem_segment_index].type;
1424 if (!VALIDATE(IsSubtypeOf(elem_type, module_->tables[imm.table.index].type,
1425 module_))) {
1426 errorf(pc, "table %u is not a super-type of %s", imm.table.index,
1427 elem_type.name().c_str());
1428 return false;
1429 }
1430 return true;
1431 }
1432
1433 inline bool Validate(const byte* pc, ElemDropImmediate<validate>& imm) {
1434 if (!VALIDATE(imm.index < module_->elem_segments.size())) {
1435 errorf(pc, "invalid element segment index: %u", imm.index);
1436 return false;
1437 }
1438 return true;
1439 }
1440
1441 inline bool Validate(const byte* pc, TableCopyImmediate<validate>& imm) {
1442 if (!Validate(pc, imm.table_src)) return false;
1443 if (!Validate(pc + imm.table_src.length, imm.table_dst)) return false;
1444 ValueType src_type = module_->tables[imm.table_src.index].type;
1445 if (!VALIDATE(IsSubtypeOf(
1446 src_type, module_->tables[imm.table_dst.index].type, module_))) {
1447 errorf(pc, "table %u is not a super-type of %s", imm.table_dst.index,
1448 src_type.name().c_str());
1449 return false;
1450 }
1451 return true;
1452 }
1453
1454 inline bool Validate(const byte* pc, HeapTypeImmediate<validate>& imm) {
1455 if (!VALIDATE(!imm.type.is_bottom())) {
1456 error(pc, "invalid heap type");
1457 return false;
1458 }
1459 if (!VALIDATE(imm.type.is_generic() ||
1460 module_->has_type(imm.type.ref_index()))) {
1461 errorf(pc, "Type index %u is out of bounds", imm.type.ref_index());
1462 return false;
1463 }
1464 return true;
1465 }
1466
1467 static uint32_t OpcodeLength(WasmDecoder* decoder, const byte* pc) {
1468 WasmOpcode opcode = static_cast<WasmOpcode>(*pc);
1469 switch (opcode) {
1470#define DECLARE_OPCODE_CASE(name, opcode, sig) case kExpr##name:
1471 FOREACH_LOAD_MEM_OPCODE(DECLARE_OPCODE_CASE)DECLARE_OPCODE_CASE(I32LoadMem, 0x28, i_i) DECLARE_OPCODE_CASE
(I64LoadMem, 0x29, l_i) DECLARE_OPCODE_CASE(F32LoadMem, 0x2a,
f_i) DECLARE_OPCODE_CASE(F64LoadMem, 0x2b, d_i) DECLARE_OPCODE_CASE
(I32LoadMem8S, 0x2c, i_i) DECLARE_OPCODE_CASE(I32LoadMem8U, 0x2d
, i_i) DECLARE_OPCODE_CASE(I32LoadMem16S, 0x2e, i_i) DECLARE_OPCODE_CASE
(I32LoadMem16U, 0x2f, i_i) DECLARE_OPCODE_CASE(I64LoadMem8S, 0x30
, l_i) DECLARE_OPCODE_CASE(I64LoadMem8U, 0x31, l_i) DECLARE_OPCODE_CASE
(I64LoadMem16S, 0x32, l_i) DECLARE_OPCODE_CASE(I64LoadMem16U,
0x33, l_i) DECLARE_OPCODE_CASE(I64LoadMem32S, 0x34, l_i) DECLARE_OPCODE_CASE
(I64LoadMem32U, 0x35, l_i)
1472 FOREACH_STORE_MEM_OPCODE(DECLARE_OPCODE_CASE)DECLARE_OPCODE_CASE(I32StoreMem, 0x36, v_ii) DECLARE_OPCODE_CASE
(I64StoreMem, 0x37, v_il) DECLARE_OPCODE_CASE(F32StoreMem, 0x38
, v_if) DECLARE_OPCODE_CASE(F64StoreMem, 0x39, v_id) DECLARE_OPCODE_CASE
(I32StoreMem8, 0x3a, v_ii) DECLARE_OPCODE_CASE(I32StoreMem16,
0x3b, v_ii) DECLARE_OPCODE_CASE(I64StoreMem8, 0x3c, v_il) DECLARE_OPCODE_CASE
(I64StoreMem16, 0x3d, v_il) DECLARE_OPCODE_CASE(I64StoreMem32
, 0x3e, v_il)
1473#undef DECLARE_OPCODE_CASE
1474 {
1475 MemoryAccessImmediate<validate> imm(decoder, pc + 1, UINT32_MAX(4294967295U));
1476 return 1 + imm.length;
1477 }
1478 case kExprBr:
1479 case kExprBrIf: {
1480 BranchDepthImmediate<validate> imm(decoder, pc + 1);
1481 return 1 + imm.length;
1482 }
1483 case kExprGlobalGet:
1484 case kExprGlobalSet: {
1485 GlobalIndexImmediate<validate> imm(decoder, pc + 1);
1486 return 1 + imm.length;
1487 }
1488 case kExprTableGet:
1489 case kExprTableSet: {
1490 TableIndexImmediate<validate> imm(decoder, pc + 1);
1491 return 1 + imm.length;
1492 }
1493 case kExprCallFunction:
1494 case kExprReturnCall: {
1495 CallFunctionImmediate<validate> imm(decoder, pc + 1);
1496 return 1 + imm.length;
1497 }
1498 case kExprCallIndirect:
1499 case kExprReturnCallIndirect: {
1500 CallIndirectImmediate<validate> imm(WasmFeatures::All(), decoder,
1501 pc + 1);
1502 return 1 + imm.length;
1503 }
1504
1505 case kExprTry:
1506 case kExprIf: // fall through
1507 case kExprLoop:
1508 case kExprBlock: {
1509 BlockTypeImmediate<validate> imm(WasmFeatures::All(), decoder, pc + 1);
1510 return 1 + imm.length;
1511 }
1512
1513 case kExprLet: {
1514 BlockTypeImmediate<validate> imm(WasmFeatures::All(), decoder, pc + 1);
1515 uint32_t locals_length;
1516 bool locals_result =
1517 decoder->DecodeLocals(decoder->pc() + 1 + imm.length,
1518 &locals_length, base::Optional<uint32_t>());
1519 return 1 + imm.length + (locals_result ? locals_length : 0);
1520 }
1521
1522 case kExprThrow: {
1523 ExceptionIndexImmediate<validate> imm(decoder, pc + 1);
1524 return 1 + imm.length;
1525 }
1526
1527 case kExprBrOnExn: {
1528 BranchOnExceptionImmediate<validate> imm(decoder, pc + 1);
1529 return 1 + imm.length;
1530 }
1531
1532 case kExprBrOnNull: {
1533 BranchDepthImmediate<validate> imm(decoder, pc + 1);
1534 return 1 + imm.length;
1535 }
1536
1537 case kExprLocalGet:
1538 case kExprLocalSet:
1539 case kExprLocalTee: {
1540 LocalIndexImmediate<validate> imm(decoder, pc + 1);
1541 return 1 + imm.length;
1542 }
1543 case kExprSelectWithType: {
1544 SelectTypeImmediate<validate> imm(WasmFeatures::All(), decoder, pc + 1);
1545 return 1 + imm.length;
1546 }
1547 case kExprBrTable: {
1548 BranchTableImmediate<validate> imm(decoder, pc + 1);
1549 BranchTableIterator<validate> iterator(decoder, imm);
1550 return 1 + iterator.length();
1551 }
1552 case kExprI32Const: {
1553 ImmI32Immediate<validate> imm(decoder, pc + 1);
1554 return 1 + imm.length;
1555 }
1556 case kExprI64Const: {
1557 ImmI64Immediate<validate> imm(decoder, pc + 1);
1558 return 1 + imm.length;
1559 }
1560 case kExprRefNull: {
1561 HeapTypeImmediate<validate> imm(WasmFeatures::All(), decoder, pc + 1);
1562 return 1 + imm.length;
1563 }
1564 case kExprRefIsNull: {
1565 return 1;
1566 }
1567 case kExprRefFunc: {
1568 FunctionIndexImmediate<validate> imm(decoder, pc + 1);
1569 return 1 + imm.length;
1570 }
1571 case kExprMemoryGrow:
1572 case kExprMemorySize: {
1573 MemoryIndexImmediate<validate> imm(decoder, pc + 1);
1574 return 1 + imm.length;
1575 }
1576 case kExprF32Const:
1577 return 5;
1578 case kExprF64Const:
1579 return 9;
1580 case kNumericPrefix: {
1581 byte numeric_index =
1582 decoder->read_u8<validate>(pc + 1, "numeric_index");
1583 WasmOpcode opcode =
1584 static_cast<WasmOpcode>(kNumericPrefix << 8 | numeric_index);
1585 switch (opcode) {
1586 case kExprI32SConvertSatF32:
1587 case kExprI32UConvertSatF32:
1588 case kExprI32SConvertSatF64:
1589 case kExprI32UConvertSatF64:
1590 case kExprI64SConvertSatF32:
1591 case kExprI64UConvertSatF32:
1592 case kExprI64SConvertSatF64:
1593 case kExprI64UConvertSatF64:
1594 return 2;
1595 case kExprMemoryInit: {
1596 MemoryInitImmediate<validate> imm(decoder, pc + 2);
1597 return 2 + imm.length;
1598 }
1599 case kExprDataDrop: {
1600 DataDropImmediate<validate> imm(decoder, pc + 2);
1601 return 2 + imm.length;
1602 }
1603 case kExprMemoryCopy: {
1604 MemoryCopyImmediate<validate> imm(decoder, pc + 2);
1605 return 2 + imm.length;
1606 }
1607 case kExprMemoryFill: {
1608 MemoryIndexImmediate<validate> imm(decoder, pc + 2);
1609 return 2 + imm.length;
1610 }
1611 case kExprTableInit: {
1612 TableInitImmediate<validate> imm(decoder, pc + 2);
1613 return 2 + imm.length;
1614 }
1615 case kExprElemDrop: {
1616 ElemDropImmediate<validate> imm(decoder, pc + 2);
1617 return 2 + imm.length;
1618 }
1619 case kExprTableCopy: {
1620 TableCopyImmediate<validate> imm(decoder, pc + 2);
1621 return 2 + imm.length;
1622 }
1623 case kExprTableGrow:
1624 case kExprTableSize:
1625 case kExprTableFill: {
1626 TableIndexImmediate<validate> imm(decoder, pc + 2);
1627 return 2 + imm.length;
1628 }
1629 default:
1630 decoder->error(pc, "invalid numeric opcode");
1631 return 2;
1632 }
1633 }
1634 case kSimdPrefix: {
1635 uint32_t length = 0;
1636 opcode = decoder->read_prefixed_opcode<validate>(pc, &length);
1637 switch (opcode) {
1638#define DECLARE_OPCODE_CASE(name, opcode, sig) case kExpr##name:
1639 FOREACH_SIMD_0_OPERAND_OPCODE(DECLARE_OPCODE_CASE)DECLARE_OPCODE_CASE(S8x16Swizzle, 0xfd0e, s_ss) DECLARE_OPCODE_CASE

, 0xfdbc, s_s) DECLARE_OPCODE_CASE(F32x4Pmin, 0xfdea, s_ss) DECLARE_OPCODE_CASE
(F32x4Pmax, 0xfdeb, s_ss) DECLARE_OPCODE_CASE(F32x4Ceil, 0xfdd8
, s_s) DECLARE_OPCODE_CASE(F32x4Floor, 0xfdd9, s_s) DECLARE_OPCODE_CASE
(F32x4Trunc, 0xfdda, s_s) DECLARE_OPCODE_CASE(F32x4NearestInt

1643 FOREACH_SIMD_1_OPERAND_OPCODE(DECLARE_OPCODE_CASE)DECLARE_OPCODE_CASE(I8x16ExtractLaneS, 0xfd15, _) DECLARE_OPCODE_CASE

(F64x2ReplaceLane, 0xfd22, _)

1646#define DECLARE_OPCODE_CASE(name, opcode, sig) case kExpr##name:
1647 FOREACH_SIMD_MEM_OPCODE(DECLARE_OPCODE_CASE)DECLARE_OPCODE_CASE(S128LoadMem, 0xfd00, s_i) DECLARE_OPCODE_CASE

1650 {
1651 MemoryAccessImmediate<validate> imm(decoder, pc + length + 1,
1652 UINT32_MAX(4294967295U));
1653 return 1 + length + imm.length;
1654 }
1655 // Shuffles require a byte per lane, or 16 immediate bytes.
1656 case kExprS128Const:
1657 case kExprS8x16Shuffle:

1659 default:

1663 }

1676#define DECLARE_OPCODE_CASE(name, opcode, sig) case kExpr##name:
1677 FOREACH_ATOMIC_0_OPERAND_OPCODE(DECLARE_OPCODE_CASE)DECLARE_OPCODE_CASE(AtomicFence, 0xfe03, v_v)

1679 {
1680 return 2 + 1;
1681 }
1682 default:
1683 decoder->error(pc, "invalid Atomics opcode");
1684 return 2;
1685 }
1686 }
1687 case kGCPrefix: {
1688 byte gc_index = decoder->read_u8<validate>(pc + 1, "gc_index");
1689 WasmOpcode opcode = static_cast<WasmOpcode>(kGCPrefix << 8 | gc_index);
1690 switch (opcode) {
1691 case kExprStructNewWithRtt:
1692 case kExprStructNewDefault: {
1693 StructIndexImmediate<validate> imm(decoder, pc + 2);
1694 return 2 + imm.length;
1695 }
1696 case kExprStructGet:
1697 case kExprStructGetS:
1698 case kExprStructGetU:
1699 case kExprStructSet: {
1700 FieldIndexImmediate<validate> imm(decoder, pc + 2);
1701 return 2 + imm.length;
1702 }
1703 case kExprArrayNewWithRtt:
1704 case kExprArrayNewDefault:
1705 case kExprArrayGet:
1706 case kExprArrayGetS:
1707 case kExprArrayGetU:
1708 case kExprArraySet:
1709 case kExprArrayLen: {
1710 ArrayIndexImmediate<validate> imm(decoder, pc + 2);
1711 return 2 + imm.length;
1712 }
1713 case kExprBrOnCast: {
1714 BranchDepthImmediate<validate> imm(decoder, pc + 2);
1715 return 2 + imm.length;
1716 }
1717 case kExprRttCanon:
1718 case kExprRttSub: {
1719 // TODO(7748): Account for rtt.sub's additional immediates if
1720 // they stick.
1721 HeapTypeImmediate<validate> imm(WasmFeatures::All(), decoder,
1722 pc + 2);
1723 return 2 + imm.length;
1724 }
1725
1726 case kExprI31New:
1727 case kExprI31GetS:
1728 case kExprI31GetU:
1729 return 2;
1730 case kExprRefTest:
1731 case kExprRefCast: {
1732 HeapTypeImmediate<validate> ht1(WasmFeatures::All(), decoder,
1733 pc + 2);
1734 HeapTypeImmediate<validate> ht2(WasmFeatures::All(), decoder,
1735 pc + 2 + ht1.length);
1736 return 2 + ht1.length + ht2.length;
1737 }
1738
1739 default:
1740 // This is unreachable except for malformed modules.
1741 decoder->error(pc, "invalid gc opcode");
1742 return 2;
1743 }
1744 }
1745 default:
1746 return 1;
1747 }
1748 }

1750 // TODO(clemensb): This is only used by the interpreter; move there.
1751 V8_EXPORT_PRIVATE std::pair<uint32_t, uint32_t> StackEffect(const byte* pc) {
1752 WasmOpcode opcode = static_cast<WasmOpcode>(*pc);
1753 // Handle "simple" opcodes with a fixed signature first.
1754 const FunctionSig* sig = WasmOpcodes::Signature(opcode);
1755 if (!sig) sig = WasmOpcodes::AsmjsSignature(opcode);
1756 if (sig) return {sig->parameter_count(), sig->return_count()};
1757
1758#define DECLARE_OPCODE_CASE(name, opcode, sig) case kExpr##name:
1759 // clang-format off
1760 switch (opcode) {
1761 case kExprSelect:
1762 case kExprSelectWithType:
1763 return {3, 1};
1764 case kExprTableSet:
1765 FOREACH_STORE_MEM_OPCODE(DECLARE_OPCODE_CASE)DECLARE_OPCODE_CASE(I32StoreMem, 0x36, v_ii) DECLARE_OPCODE_CASE
(I64StoreMem, 0x37, v_il) DECLARE_OPCODE_CASE(F32StoreMem, 0x38
, v_if) DECLARE_OPCODE_CASE(F64StoreMem, 0x39, v_id) DECLARE_OPCODE_CASE
(I32StoreMem8, 0x3a, v_ii) DECLARE_OPCODE_CASE(I32StoreMem16,
0x3b, v_ii) DECLARE_OPCODE_CASE(I64StoreMem8, 0x3c, v_il) DECLARE_OPCODE_CASE
(I64StoreMem16, 0x3d, v_il) DECLARE_OPCODE_CASE(I64StoreMem32
, 0x3e, v_il)
1766 return {2, 0};
1767 FOREACH_LOAD_MEM_OPCODE(DECLARE_OPCODE_CASE)DECLARE_OPCODE_CASE(I32LoadMem, 0x28, i_i) DECLARE_OPCODE_CASE
(I64LoadMem, 0x29, l_i) DECLARE_OPCODE_CASE(F32LoadMem, 0x2a,
f_i) DECLARE_OPCODE_CASE(F64LoadMem, 0x2b, d_i) DECLARE_OPCODE_CASE
(I32LoadMem8S, 0x2c, i_i) DECLARE_OPCODE_CASE(I32LoadMem8U, 0x2d
, i_i) DECLARE_OPCODE_CASE(I32LoadMem16S, 0x2e, i_i) DECLARE_OPCODE_CASE
(I32LoadMem16U, 0x2f, i_i) DECLARE_OPCODE_CASE(I64LoadMem8S, 0x30
, l_i) DECLARE_OPCODE_CASE(I64LoadMem8U, 0x31, l_i) DECLARE_OPCODE_CASE
(I64LoadMem16S, 0x32, l_i) DECLARE_OPCODE_CASE(I64LoadMem16U,
0x33, l_i) DECLARE_OPCODE_CASE(I64LoadMem32S, 0x34, l_i) DECLARE_OPCODE_CASE
(I64LoadMem32U, 0x35, l_i)
1768 case kExprTableGet:
1769 case kExprLocalTee:
1770 case kExprMemoryGrow:
1771 case kExprRefAsNonNull:
1772 case kExprBrOnNull:
1773 case kExprRefIsNull:
1774 return {1, 1};
1775 case kExprLocalSet:
1776 case kExprGlobalSet:
1777 case kExprDrop:
1778 case kExprBrIf:
1779 case kExprBrTable:
1780 case kExprIf:
1781 case kExprRethrow:
1782 return {1, 0};
1783 case kExprLocalGet:
1784 case kExprGlobalGet:
1785 case kExprI32Const:
1786 case kExprI64Const:
1787 case kExprF32Const:
1788 case kExprF64Const:
1789 case kExprRefNull:
1790 case kExprRefFunc:
1791 case kExprMemorySize:
1792 return {0, 1};
1793 case kExprCallFunction: {
1794 CallFunctionImmediate<validate> imm(this, pc + 1);
1795 CHECK(Complete(imm))do { if ((__builtin_expect(!!(!(Complete(imm))), 0))) { V8_Fatal
("Check failed: %s.", "Complete(imm)"); } } while (false);
1796 return {imm.sig->parameter_count(), imm.sig->return_count()};
1797 }
1798 case kExprCallIndirect: {
1799 CallIndirectImmediate<validate> imm(this->enabled_, this, pc + 1);
1800 CHECK(Complete(imm))do { if ((__builtin_expect(!!(!(Complete(imm))), 0))) { V8_Fatal
("Check failed: %s.", "Complete(imm)"); } } while (false);
1801 // Indirect calls pop an additional argument for the table index.
1802 return {imm.sig->parameter_count() + 1,
1803 imm.sig->return_count()};
1804 }
1805 case kExprThrow: {
1806 ExceptionIndexImmediate<validate> imm(this, pc + 1);
1807 CHECK(Complete(imm))do { if ((__builtin_expect(!!(!(Complete(imm))), 0))) { V8_Fatal
("Check failed: %s.", "Complete(imm)"); } } while (false);
1808 DCHECK_EQ(0, imm.exception->sig->return_count())((void) 0);
1809 return {imm.exception->sig->parameter_count(), 0};
1810 }
1811 case kExprBr:
1812 case kExprBlock:
1813 case kExprLoop:
1814 case kExprEnd:
1815 case kExprElse:
1816 case kExprTry:
1817 case kExprCatch:
1818 case kExprBrOnExn:
1819 case kExprNop:
1820 case kExprReturn:
1821 case kExprReturnCall:
1822 case kExprReturnCallIndirect:
1823 case kExprUnreachable:
1824 return {0, 0};
1825 case kExprLet:
1826 // TODO(7748): Implement
1827 return {0, 0};
1828 case kNumericPrefix:
1829 case kAtomicPrefix:
1830 case kSimdPrefix: {
1831 opcode = this->read_prefixed_opcode<validate>(pc);
1832 switch (opcode) {
1833 FOREACH_SIMD_1_OPERAND_1_PARAM_OPCODE(DECLARE_OPCODE_CASE)DECLARE_OPCODE_CASE(I8x16ExtractLaneS, 0xfd15, _) DECLARE_OPCODE_CASE
(I8x16ExtractLaneU, 0xfd16, _) DECLARE_OPCODE_CASE(I16x8ExtractLaneS
, 0xfd18, _) DECLARE_OPCODE_CASE(I16x8ExtractLaneU, 0xfd19, _
) DECLARE_OPCODE_CASE(I32x4ExtractLane, 0xfd1b, _) DECLARE_OPCODE_CASE
(I64x2ExtractLane, 0xfd1d, _) DECLARE_OPCODE_CASE(F32x4ExtractLane
, 0xfd1f, _) DECLARE_OPCODE_CASE(F64x2ExtractLane, 0xfd21, _)
1834 return {1, 1};
1835 FOREACH_SIMD_1_OPERAND_2_PARAM_OPCODE(DECLARE_OPCODE_CASE)DECLARE_OPCODE_CASE(I8x16ReplaceLane, 0xfd17, _) DECLARE_OPCODE_CASE
(I16x8ReplaceLane, 0xfd1a, _) DECLARE_OPCODE_CASE(I32x4ReplaceLane
, 0xfd1c, _) DECLARE_OPCODE_CASE(I64x2ReplaceLane, 0xfd1e, _)
DECLARE_OPCODE_CASE(F32x4ReplaceLane, 0xfd20, _) DECLARE_OPCODE_CASE
(F64x2ReplaceLane, 0xfd22, _)
1836 FOREACH_SIMD_MASK_OPERAND_OPCODE(DECLARE_OPCODE_CASE)DECLARE_OPCODE_CASE(S8x16Shuffle, 0xfd0d, s_ss)
1837 return {2, 1};
1838 FOREACH_SIMD_CONST_OPCODE(DECLARE_OPCODE_CASE)DECLARE_OPCODE_CASE(S128Const, 0xfd0c, _)
1839 return {0, 1};
1840 default: {
1841 sig = WasmOpcodes::Signature(opcode);
1842 if (sig) {
1843 return {sig->parameter_count(), sig->return_count()};
1844 } else {
1845 UNREACHABLE()V8_Fatal("unreachable code");
1846 }
1847 }
1848 }
1849 }
1850 case kGCPrefix: {
1851 opcode = this->read_prefixed_opcode<validate>(pc);
1852 switch (opcode) {
1853 case kExprStructNewDefault:
1854 case kExprStructGet:
1855 case kExprStructGetS:
1856 case kExprStructGetU:
1857 case kExprI31New:
1858 case kExprI31GetS:
1859 case kExprI31GetU:
1860 case kExprArrayLen:
1861 case kExprRttSub:
1862 return {1, 1};
1863 case kExprStructSet:
1864 return {2, 0};
1865 case kExprArrayNewDefault:
1866 case kExprArrayGet:
1867 case kExprArrayGetS:
1868 case kExprArrayGetU:
1869 case kExprRefTest:
1870 case kExprRefCast:
1871 case kExprBrOnCast:
1872 return {2, 1};
1873 case kExprArraySet:
1874 return {3, 0};
1875 case kExprRttCanon:
1876 return {0, 1};
1877 case kExprArrayNewWithRtt:
1878 return {3, 1};
1879 case kExprStructNewWithRtt: {
1880 StructIndexImmediate<validate> imm(this, this->pc_ + 2);
1881 this->Complete(imm);
1882 return {imm.struct_type->field_count() + 1, 1};
1883 }
1884 default:
1885 UNREACHABLE()V8_Fatal("unreachable code");
1886 }
1887 }
1888 default:
1889 FATAL("unimplemented opcode: %x (%s)", opcode,V8_Fatal("unimplemented opcode: %x (%s)", opcode, WasmOpcodes
::OpcodeName(opcode))
1890 WasmOpcodes::OpcodeName(opcode))V8_Fatal("unimplemented opcode: %x (%s)", opcode, WasmOpcodes
::OpcodeName(opcode));
1891 return {0, 0};
1892 }
1893#undef DECLARE_OPCODE_CASE
1894 // clang-format on
1895 }
1896
1897 // The {Zone} is implicitly stored in the {ZoneAllocator} which is part of
1898 // this {ZoneVector}. Hence save one field and just get it from there if
1899 // needed (see {zone()} accessor below).
1900 ZoneVector<ValueType> local_types_;
1901
1902 const WasmModule* module_;
1903 const WasmFeatures enabled_;
1904 WasmFeatures* detected_;
1905 const FunctionSig* sig_;
1906};
1907
1908#define CALL_INTERFACE(name, ...) interface_.name(this, ##__VA_ARGS__)
1909#define CALL_INTERFACE_IF_REACHABLE(name, ...) \
1910 do { \
1911 DCHECK(!control_.empty())((void) 0); \
1912 DCHECK_EQ(current_code_reachable_, \((void) 0)
1913 this->ok() && control_.back().reachable())((void) 0); \
1914 if (current_code_reachable_) { \
1915 interface_.name(this, ##__VA_ARGS__); \
1916 } \
1917 } while (false)
1918#define CALL_INTERFACE_IF_PARENT_REACHABLE(name, ...) \
1919 do { \
1920 DCHECK(!control_.empty())((void) 0); \
1921 if (VALIDATE(this->ok()) && \
1922 (control_.size() == 1 || control_at(1)->reachable())) { \
1923 interface_.name(this, ##__VA_ARGS__); \
1924 } \
1925 } while (false)
1926
1927template <Decoder::ValidateFlag validate, typename Interface>
1928class WasmFullDecoder : public WasmDecoder<validate> {
1929 using Value = typename Interface::Value;
1930 using Control = typename Interface::Control;
1931 using ArgVector = base::SmallVector<Value, 8>;
1932
1933 // All Value types should be trivially copyable for performance. We push, pop,
1934 // and store them in local variables.
1935 ASSERT_TRIVIALLY_COPYABLE(Value)static_assert(::v8::base::is_trivially_copyable<Value>::
value, "Value" " should be trivially copyable");
1936
1937 public:
1938 template <typename... InterfaceArgs>
1939 WasmFullDecoder(Zone* zone, const WasmModule* module,
1940 const WasmFeatures& enabled, WasmFeatures* detected,
1941 const FunctionBody& body, InterfaceArgs&&... interface_args)
1942 : WasmDecoder<validate>(zone, module, enabled, detected, body.sig,
1943 body.start, body.end, body.offset),
1944 interface_(std::forward<InterfaceArgs>(interface_args)...),
1945 stack_(zone),
1946 control_(zone) {}
1947
1948 Interface& interface() { return interface_; }
1949
1950 bool Decode() {
1951 DCHECK(stack_.empty())((void) 0);
1952 DCHECK(control_.empty())((void) 0);
1953 DCHECK_LE(this->pc_, this->end_)((void) 0);
1954 DCHECK_EQ(this->num_locals(), 0)((void) 0);
1955
1956 this->InitializeLocalsFromSig();
1957 uint32_t params_count = static_cast<uint32_t>(this->num_locals());
1958 uint32_t locals_length;
1959 this->DecodeLocals(this->pc(), &locals_length, params_count);
1960 for (uint32_t index = params_count; index < this->num_locals(); index++) {
1961 if (!VALIDATE(this->local_type(index).is_defaultable())) {
1962 this->errorf(
1963 this->pc(),
1964 "Cannot define function-level local of non-defaultable type %s",
1965 this->local_type(index).name().c_str());
1966 }
1967 }
1968 this->consume_bytes(locals_length);
1969
1970 CALL_INTERFACE(StartFunction);
1971 DecodeFunctionBody();
1972 if (!this->failed()) CALL_INTERFACE(FinishFunction);
1973
1974 // Generate a better error message whether the unterminated control
1975 // structure is the function body block or an innner structure.
1976 if (!VALIDATE(control_.empty())) {
1977 if (control_.size() > 1) {
1978 this->error(control_.back().pc, "unterminated control structure");
1979 } else if (control_.size() == 1) {
1980 this->error("function body must end with \"end\" opcode");
1981 }
1982 }
1983
1984 if (!VALIDATE(this->ok())) return this->TraceFailed();
1985
1986 TRACE("wasm-decode %s\n\n", VALIDATE(this->ok()) ? "ok" : "failed");
1987
1988 return true;
1989 }
1990
1991 bool TraceFailed() {
1992 TRACE("wasm-error module+%-6d func+%d: %s\n\n", this->error_.offset(),
1993 this->GetBufferRelativeOffset(this->error_.offset()),
1994 this->error_.message().c_str());
1995 return false;
1996 }
1997
1998 const char* SafeOpcodeNameAt(const byte* pc) {
1999 if (pc >= this->end_) return "<end>";
2000 WasmOpcode opcode = static_cast<WasmOpcode>(*pc);
2001 if (!WasmOpcodes::IsPrefixOpcode(opcode)) {
2002 return WasmOpcodes::OpcodeName(static_cast<WasmOpcode>(opcode));
2003 }
2004 opcode = this->template read_prefixed_opcode<Decoder::kValidate>(pc);
2005 return WasmOpcodes::OpcodeName(opcode);
2006 }
2007
2008 inline WasmCodePosition position() {
2009 int offset = static_cast<int>(this->pc_ - this->start_);
2010 DCHECK_EQ(this->pc_ - this->start_, offset)((void) 0); // overflows cannot happen
2011 return offset;
2012 }
2013
2014 inline uint32_t control_depth() const {
2015 return static_cast<uint32_t>(control_.size());
2016 }
2017
2018 inline Control* control_at(uint32_t depth) {
2019 DCHECK_GT(control_.size(), depth)((void) 0);
2020 return &control_.back() - depth;
2021 }
2022
2023 inline uint32_t stack_size() const {
2024 DCHECK_GE(kMaxUInt32, stack_.size())((void) 0);
2025 return static_cast<uint32_t>(stack_.size());
2026 }
2027
2028 inline Value* stack_value(uint32_t depth) {
2029 DCHECK_LT(0, depth)((void) 0);
2030 DCHECK_GE(stack_.size(), depth)((void) 0);
2031 return &*(stack_.end() - depth);
2032 }
2033
2034 void SetSucceedingCodeDynamicallyUnreachable() {
2035 Control* current = &control_.back();
2036 if (current->reachable()) {
2037 current->reachability = kSpecOnlyReachable;
2038 current_code_reachable_ = false;
2039 }
2040 }
2041
2042 private:
2043 Interface interface_;
2044
2045 ZoneVector<Value> stack_; // stack of values.
2046 ZoneVector<Control> control_; // stack of blocks, loops, and ifs.
2047 // Controls whether code should be generated for the current block (basically
2048 // a cache for {ok() && control_.back().reachable()}).
2049 bool current_code_reachable_ = true;
2050
2051 static Value UnreachableValue(const uint8_t* pc) {
2052 return Value{pc, kWasmBottom};
2053 }
2054
2055 bool CheckHasMemory() {
2056 if (!VALIDATE(this->module_->has_memory)) {
2057 this->error(this->pc_ - 1, "memory instruction with no memory");
2058 return false;
2059 }
2060 return true;
2061 }
2062
2063 bool CheckHasMemoryForAtomics() {
2064 if (FLAG_wasm_atomics_on_non_shared_memory && CheckHasMemory()) return true;
2065 if (!VALIDATE(this->module_->has_shared_memory)) {
2066 this->error(this->pc_ - 1, "Atomic opcodes used without shared memory");
2067 return false;
2068 }
2069 return true;
2070 }
2071
2072 bool CheckSimdPostMvp(WasmOpcode opcode) {
2073 if (!FLAG_wasm_simd_post_mvp && WasmOpcodes::IsSimdPostMvpOpcode(opcode)) {
2074 this->error(
2075 "simd opcode not available, enable with --wasm-simd-post-mvp");
2076 return false;
2077 }
2078 return true;
2079 }
2080
2081#ifdef DEBUG
2082 class TraceLine {
2083 public:
2084 explicit TraceLine(WasmFullDecoder* decoder) : decoder_(decoder) {
2085 WasmOpcode opcode = static_cast<WasmOpcode>(*decoder->pc());
2086 if (!WasmOpcodes::IsPrefixOpcode(opcode)) AppendOpcode(opcode);
2087 }
2088
2089 void AppendOpcode(WasmOpcode opcode) {
2090 DCHECK(!WasmOpcodes::IsPrefixOpcode(opcode))((void) 0);
2091 Append(TRACE_INST_FORMAT, decoder_->startrel(decoder_->pc_),
2092 WasmOpcodes::OpcodeName(opcode));
2093 }
2094
2095 ~TraceLine() {
2096 if (!FLAG_trace_wasm_decoder) return;
2097 AppendStackState();
2098 PrintF("%.*s\n", len_, buffer_);
2099 }
2100
2101 // Appends a formatted string.
2102 PRINTF_FORMAT(2, 3)__attribute__((format(printf, 2, 3)))
2103 void Append(const char* format, ...) {
2104 if (!FLAG_trace_wasm_decoder) return;
2105 va_list va_args;
2106 va_start(va_args, format)__builtin_va_start(va_args, format);
2107 size_t remaining_len = kMaxLen - len_;
2108 Vector<char> remaining_msg_space(buffer_ + len_, remaining_len);
2109 int len = VSNPrintF(remaining_msg_space, format, va_args);
2110 va_end(va_args)__builtin_va_end(va_args);
2111 len_ += len < 0 ? remaining_len : len;
2112 }
2113
2114 private:
2115 void AppendStackState() {
2116 DCHECK(FLAG_trace_wasm_decoder)((void) 0);
2117 Append(" ");
2118 for (Control& c : decoder_->control_) {
2119 switch (c.kind) {
2120 case kControlIf:
2121 Append("I");
2122 break;
2123 case kControlBlock:
2124 Append("B");
2125 break;
2126 case kControlLoop:
2127 Append("L");
2128 break;
2129 case kControlTry:
2130 Append("T");
2131 break;
2132 case kControlIfElse:
2133 case kControlTryCatch:
2134 case kControlLet: // TODO(7748): Implement
2135 break;
2136 }
2137 if (c.start_merge.arity) Append("%u-", c.start_merge.arity);
2138 Append("%u", c.end_merge.arity);
2139 if (!c.reachable()) Append("%c", c.unreachable() ? '*' : '#');
2140 }
2141 Append(" | ");
2142 for (size_t i = 0; i < decoder_->stack_.size(); ++i) {
2143 Value& val = decoder_->stack_[i];
2144 WasmOpcode val_opcode = static_cast<WasmOpcode>(*val.pc);
2145 if (WasmOpcodes::IsPrefixOpcode(val_opcode)) {
2146 val_opcode =
2147 decoder_->template read_prefixed_opcode<Decoder::kNoValidate>(
2148 val.pc);
2149 }
2150 Append(" %c@%d:%s", val.type.short_name(),
2151 static_cast<int>(val.pc - decoder_->start_),
2152 WasmOpcodes::OpcodeName(val_opcode));
2153 // If the decoder failed, don't try to decode the immediates, as this
2154 // can trigger a DCHECK failure.
2155 if (decoder_->failed()) continue;
2156 switch (val_opcode) {
2157 case kExprI32Const: {
2158 ImmI32Immediate<Decoder::kNoValidate> imm(decoder_, val.pc + 1);
2159 Append("[%d]", imm.value);
2160 break;
2161 }
2162 case kExprLocalGet:
2163 case kExprLocalSet:
2164 case kExprLocalTee: {
2165 LocalIndexImmediate<Decoder::kNoValidate> imm(decoder_, val.pc + 1);
2166 Append("[%u]", imm.index);
2167 break;
2168 }
2169 case kExprGlobalGet:
2170 case kExprGlobalSet: {
2171 GlobalIndexImmediate<Decoder::kNoValidate> imm(decoder_,
2172 val.pc + 1);
2173 Append("[%u]", imm.index);
2174 break;
2175 }
2176 default:
2177 break;
2178 }
2179 }
2180 }
2181
2182 static constexpr int kMaxLen = 512;
2183
2184 char buffer_[kMaxLen];
2185 int len_ = 0;
2186 WasmFullDecoder* const decoder_;
2187 };
2188#else
2189 class TraceLine {
2190 public:
2191 explicit TraceLine(WasmFullDecoder*) {}
2192
2193 void AppendOpcode(WasmOpcode) {}
2194
2195 PRINTF_FORMAT(2, 3)__attribute__((format(printf, 2, 3)))
2196 void Append(const char* format, ...) {}
2197 };
2198#endif

2203 return decoder->Decode##name##Impl(&trace_msg, opcode); \
2204 } \
2205 V8_INLINEinline __attribute__((always_inline)) int Decode##name##Impl(TraceLine* trace_msg, WasmOpcode opcode)
2206
2207 DECODE(Nop) { return 1; }

2214 DECODE(Block) {
2215 BlockTypeImmediate<validate> imm(this->enabled_, this, this->pc_ + 1);
2216 if (!this->Validate(this->pc_ + 1, imm)) return 0;
2217 ArgVector args = PopArgs(imm.sig);
2218 Control* block = PushControl(kControlBlock);
2219 SetBlockType(block, imm, args.begin());
2220 CALL_INTERFACE_IF_REACHABLE(Block, block);
2221 PushMergeValues(block, &block->start_merge);
2222 return 1 + imm.length;
2223 }
2224
2225 DECODE(Rethrow) {
2226 CHECK_PROTOTYPE_OPCODE(eh);
2227 Value exception = Pop(0, kWasmExnRef);
2228 CALL_INTERFACE_IF_REACHABLE(Rethrow, exception);
2229 EndControl();
2230 return 1;
2231 }
2232
2233 DECODE(Throw) {
2234 CHECK_PROTOTYPE_OPCODE(eh);
2235 ExceptionIndexImmediate<validate> imm(this, this->pc_ + 1);
2236 if (!this->Validate(this->pc_ + 1, imm)) return 0;
2237 ArgVector args = PopArgs(imm.exception->ToFunctionSig());
2238 CALL_INTERFACE_IF_REACHABLE(Throw, imm, VectorOf(args));
2239 EndControl();
2240 return 1 + imm.length;
2241 }
2242
2243 DECODE(Try) {
2244 CHECK_PROTOTYPE_OPCODE(eh);
2245 BlockTypeImmediate<validate> imm(this->enabled_, this, this->pc_ + 1);
2246 if (!this->Validate(this->pc_ + 1, imm)) return 0;
2247 ArgVector args = PopArgs(imm.sig);
2248 Control* try_block = PushControl(kControlTry);
2249 SetBlockType(try_block, imm, args.begin());
2250 CALL_INTERFACE_IF_REACHABLE(Try, try_block);
2251 PushMergeValues(try_block, &try_block->start_merge);
2252 return 1 + imm.length;
2253 }
2254
2255 DECODE(Catch) {
2256 CHECK_PROTOTYPE_OPCODE(eh);
2257 if (!VALIDATE(!control_.empty())) {
2258 this->error("catch does not match any try");
2259 return 0;
2260 }
2261 Control* c = &control_.back();
2262 if (!VALIDATE(c->is_try())) {
2263 this->error("catch does not match any try");
2264 return 0;
2265 }
2266 if (!VALIDATE(c->is_incomplete_try())) {
2267 this->error("catch already present for try");
2268 return 0;
2269 }
2270 c->kind = kControlTryCatch;
2271 FallThruTo(c);
2272 stack_.erase(stack_.begin() + c->stack_depth, stack_.end());
2273 c->reachability = control_at(1)->innerReachability();
2274 current_code_reachable_ = this->ok() && c->reachable();
2275 Value* exception = Push(kWasmExnRef);
2276 CALL_INTERFACE_IF_PARENT_REACHABLE(Catch, c, exception);
2277 return 1;
2278 }
2279
2280 DECODE(BrOnExn) {
2281 CHECK_PROTOTYPE_OPCODE(eh);
2282 BranchOnExceptionImmediate<validate> imm(this, this->pc_ + 1);
2283 if (!this->Validate(this->pc() + 1, imm, control_.size())) return 0;
2284 Control* c = control_at(imm.depth.depth);
2285 Value exception = Pop(0, kWasmExnRef);
2286 const WasmExceptionSig* sig = imm.index.exception->sig;
2287 size_t value_count = sig->parameter_count();
2288 // TODO(wasm): This operand stack mutation is an ugly hack to make
2289 // both type checking here as well as environment merging in the
2290 // graph builder interface work out of the box. We should introduce
2291 // special handling for both and do minimal/no stack mutation here.
2292 for (size_t i = 0; i < value_count; ++i) Push(sig->GetParam(i));
2293 Vector<Value> values(stack_.data() + c->stack_depth, value_count);
2294 TypeCheckBranchResult check_result = TypeCheckBranch(c, true);
2295 if (this->failed()) return 0;
2296 if (V8_LIKELY(check_result == kReachableBranch)(__builtin_expect(!!(check_result == kReachableBranch), 1))) {
2297 CALL_INTERFACE(BrOnException, exception, imm.index, imm.depth.depth,
2298 values);
2299 c->br_merge()->reached = true;
2300 } else if (check_result == kInvalidStack) {
2301 return 0;
2302 }
2303 for (int i = static_cast<int>(value_count) - 1; i >= 0; i--) Pop(i);
2304 Value* pexception = Push(kWasmExnRef);
2305 *pexception = exception;
2306 return 1 + imm.length;
2307 }
2308
2309 DECODE(BrOnNull) {
2310 CHECK_PROTOTYPE_OPCODE(typed_funcref);
2311 BranchDepthImmediate<validate> imm(this, this->pc_ + 1);
2312 if (!this->Validate(this->pc_ + 1, imm, control_.size())) return 0;
2313 Value ref_object = Pop(0);
2314 if (this->failed()) return 0;
2315 Control* c = control_at(imm.depth);
2316 TypeCheckBranchResult check_result = TypeCheckBranch(c, true);
2317 if (V8_LIKELY(check_result == kReachableBranch)(__builtin_expect(!!(check_result == kReachableBranch), 1))) {
2318 switch (ref_object.type.kind()) {
2319 case ValueType::kRef: {
2320 Value* result = Push(ref_object.type);
2321 CALL_INTERFACE(PassThrough, ref_object, result);
2322 break;
2323 }
2324 case ValueType::kOptRef: {
2325 // We need to Push the result value after calling BrOnNull on
2326 // the interface. Therefore we must sync the ref_object and
2327 // result nodes afterwards (in PassThrough).
2328 CALL_INTERFACE(BrOnNull, ref_object, imm.depth);
2329 Value* result =
2330 Push(ValueType::Ref(ref_object.type.heap_type(), kNonNullable));
2331 CALL_INTERFACE(PassThrough, ref_object, result);
2332 c->br_merge()->reached = true;
2333 break;
2334 }
2335 default:
2336 this->error(this->pc_, "invalid argument type to br_on_null");
2337 return 0;
2338 }
2339 } else if (check_result == kInvalidStack) {
2340 return 0;
2341 }
2342 return 1 + imm.length;
2343 }
2344
2345 DECODE(Let) {
2346 CHECK_PROTOTYPE_OPCODE(typed_funcref);
2347 BlockTypeImmediate<validate> imm(this->enabled_, this, this->pc_ + 1);
2348 if (!this->Validate(this->pc_ + 1, imm)) return 0;
2349 uint32_t old_local_count = this->num_locals();
2350 // Temporarily add the let-defined values
2351 // to the beginning of the function locals.
2352 uint32_t locals_length;
2353 if (!this->DecodeLocals(this->pc() + 1 + imm.length, &locals_length, 0)) {
2354 return 0;
2355 }
2356 uint32_t num_added_locals = this->num_locals() - old_local_count;
2357 ArgVector let_local_values =
2358 PopArgs(static_cast<uint32_t>(imm.in_arity()),
2359 VectorOf(this->local_types_.data(), num_added_locals));
2360 ArgVector args = PopArgs(imm.sig);
2361 Control* let_block = PushControl(kControlLet, num_added_locals);
2362 SetBlockType(let_block, imm, args.begin());
2363 CALL_INTERFACE_IF_REACHABLE(Block, let_block);
2364 PushMergeValues(let_block, &let_block->start_merge);
2365 CALL_INTERFACE_IF_REACHABLE(AllocateLocals, VectorOf(let_local_values));
2366 return 1 + imm.length + locals_length;
2367 }
2368
2369 DECODE(Loop) {
2370 BlockTypeImmediate<validate> imm(this->enabled_, this, this->pc_ + 1);
2371 if (!this->Validate(this->pc_ + 1, imm)) return 0;
2372 ArgVector args = PopArgs(imm.sig);
2373 Control* block = PushControl(kControlLoop);
2374 SetBlockType(&control_.back(), imm, args.begin());
2375 CALL_INTERFACE_IF_REACHABLE(Loop, block);
2376 PushMergeValues(block, &block->start_merge);
2377 return 1 + imm.length;
2378 }
2379
2380 DECODE(If) {
2381 BlockTypeImmediate<validate> imm(this->enabled_, this, this->pc_ + 1);
2382 if (!this->Validate(this->pc_ + 1, imm)) return 0;
2383 Value cond = Pop(0, kWasmI32);
2384 ArgVector args = PopArgs(imm.sig);
2385 if (!VALIDATE(this->ok())) return 0;
2386 Control* if_block = PushControl(kControlIf);
2387 SetBlockType(if_block, imm, args.begin());
2388 CALL_INTERFACE_IF_REACHABLE(If, cond, if_block);
2389 PushMergeValues(if_block, &if_block->start_merge);
2390 return 1 + imm.length;
2391 }
2392
2393 DECODE(Else) {
2394 if (!VALIDATE(!control_.empty())) {
2395 this->error("else does not match any if");
2396 return 0;
2397 }
2398 Control* c = &control_.back();
2399 if (!VALIDATE(c->is_if())) {
2400 this->error(this->pc_, "else does not match an if");
2401 return 0;
2402 }
2403 if (!VALIDATE(c->is_onearmed_if())) {
2404 this->error(this->pc_, "else already present for if");
2405 return 0;
2406 }
2407 if (!TypeCheckFallThru()) return 0;
2408 c->kind = kControlIfElse;
2409 CALL_INTERFACE_IF_PARENT_REACHABLE(Else, c);
2410 if (c->reachable()) c->end_merge.reached = true;
2411 PushMergeValues(c, &c->start_merge);
2412 c->reachability = control_at(1)->innerReachability();
2413 current_code_reachable_ = this->ok() && c->reachable();
2414 return 1;
2415 }
2416
2417 DECODE(End) {
2418 if (!VALIDATE(!control_.empty())) {
2419 this->error("end does not match any if, try, or block");
2420 return 0;
2421 }
2422 Control* c = &control_.back();
2423 if (!VALIDATE(!c->is_incomplete_try())) {
2424 this->error(this->pc_, "missing catch or catch-all in try");
2425 return 0;
2426 }
2427 if (c->is_onearmed_if()) {
2428 if (!VALIDATE(c->end_merge.arity == c->start_merge.arity)) {
2429 this->error(c->pc,
2430 "start-arity and end-arity of one-armed if must match");
2431 return 0;
2432 }
2433 if (!TypeCheckOneArmedIf(c)) return 0;
2434 }
2435 if (c->is_let()) {
2436 this->local_types_.erase(this->local_types_.begin(),
2437 this->local_types_.begin() + c->locals_count);
2438 CALL_INTERFACE_IF_REACHABLE(DeallocateLocals, c->locals_count);
2439 }
2440 if (!TypeCheckFallThru()) return 0;
2441
2442 if (control_.size() == 1) {
2443 // If at the last (implicit) control, check we are at end.
2444 if (!VALIDATE(this->pc_ + 1 == this->end_)) {
2445 this->error(this->pc_ + 1, "trailing code after function end");
2446 return 0;
2447 }
2448 // The result of the block is the return value.
2449 trace_msg->Append("\n" TRACE_INST_FORMAT, startrel(this->pc_),
2450 "(implicit) return");
2451 DoReturn();
2452 control_.clear();
2453 return 1;
2454 }
2455 PopControl(c);
2456 return 1;
2457 }
2458
2459 DECODE(Select) {
2460 Value cond = Pop(2, kWasmI32);
2461 Value fval = Pop(1);
2462 Value tval = Pop(0, fval.type);
2463 ValueType type = tval.type == kWasmBottom ? fval.type : tval.type;
2464 if (!VALIDATE(!type.is_reference_type())) {
2465 this->error("select without type is only valid for value type inputs");
2466 return 0;
2467 }
2468 Value* result = Push(type);
2469 CALL_INTERFACE_IF_REACHABLE(Select, cond, fval, tval, result);
2470 return 1;
2471 }
2472
2473 DECODE(SelectWithType) {
2474 CHECK_PROTOTYPE_OPCODE(reftypes);
2475 SelectTypeImmediate<validate> imm(this->enabled_, this, this->pc_ + 1);
2476 if (this->failed()) return 0;
2477 Value cond = Pop(2, kWasmI32);
2478 Value fval = Pop(1, imm.type);
2479 Value tval = Pop(0, imm.type);
2480 Value* result = Push(imm.type);
2481 CALL_INTERFACE_IF_REACHABLE(Select, cond, fval, tval, result);
2482 return 1 + imm.length;
2483 }
2484
2485 DECODE(Br) {
2486 BranchDepthImmediate<validate> imm(this, this->pc_ + 1);
2487 if (!this->Validate(this->pc_ + 1, imm, control_.size())) return 0;
2488 Control* c = control_at(imm.depth);
2489 TypeCheckBranchResult check_result = TypeCheckBranch(c, false);
2490 if (V8_LIKELY(check_result == kReachableBranch)(__builtin_expect(!!(check_result == kReachableBranch), 1))) {
2491 if (imm.depth == control_.size() - 1) {
2492 DoReturn();
2493 } else {
2494 CALL_INTERFACE(Br, c);
2495 c->br_merge()->reached = true;
2496 }
2497 } else if (check_result == kInvalidStack) {
2498 return 0;
2499 }
2500 EndControl();
2501 return 1 + imm.length;
2502 }
2503
2504 DECODE(BrIf) {
2505 BranchDepthImmediate<validate> imm(this, this->pc_ + 1);
2506 if (!this->Validate(this->pc_ + 1, imm, control_.size())) return 0;
2507 Value cond = Pop(0, kWasmI32);
2508 if (this->failed()) return 0;
2509 Control* c = control_at(imm.depth);
2510 TypeCheckBranchResult check_result = TypeCheckBranch(c, true);
2511 if (V8_LIKELY(check_result == kReachableBranch)(__builtin_expect(!!(check_result == kReachableBranch), 1))) {
2512 CALL_INTERFACE(BrIf, cond, imm.depth);
2513 c->br_merge()->reached = true;
2514 } else if (check_result == kInvalidStack) {
2515 return 0;
2516 }
2517 return 1 + imm.length;
2518 }
2519
2520 DECODE(BrTable) {
2521 BranchTableImmediate<validate> imm(this, this->pc_ + 1);
2522 BranchTableIterator<validate> iterator(this, imm);
2523 Value key = Pop(0, kWasmI32);
2524 if (this->failed()) return 0;
2525 if (!this->Validate(this->pc_ + 1, imm, control_.size())) return 0;
2526
2527 // Cache the branch targets during the iteration, so that we can set
2528 // all branch targets as reachable after the {CALL_INTERFACE} call.
2529 std::vector<bool> br_targets(control_.size());
2530
2531 // The result types of the br_table instruction. We have to check the
2532 // stack against these types. Only needed during validation.
2533 std::vector<ValueType> result_types;
2534
2535 while (iterator.has_next()) {
2536 const uint32_t index = iterator.cur_index();
2537 const byte* pos = iterator.pc();
2538 uint32_t target = iterator.next();
2539 if (!VALIDATE(ValidateBrTableTarget(target, pos, index))) return 0;
2540 // Avoid redundant branch target checks.
2541 if (br_targets[target]) continue;
2542 br_targets[target] = true;
2543
2544 if (validate) {
2545 if (index == 0) {
2546 // With the first branch target, initialize the result types.
2547 result_types = InitializeBrTableResultTypes(target);
2548 } else if (!UpdateBrTableResultTypes(&result_types, target, pos,
2549 index)) {
2550 return 0;
2551 }
2552 }
2553 }
2554
2555 if (!VALIDATE(TypeCheckBrTable(result_types))) return 0;
2556
2557 DCHECK(this->ok())((void) 0);
2558
2559 if (current_code_reachable_) {
2560 CALL_INTERFACE(BrTable, imm, key);
2561
2562 for (int i = 0, e = control_depth(); i < e; ++i) {
2563 if (!br_targets[i]) continue;
2564 control_at(i)->br_merge()->reached = true;
2565 }
2566 }
2567
2568 EndControl();
2569 return 1 + iterator.length();
2570 }
2571
2572 DECODE(Return) {
2573 if (V8_LIKELY(current_code_reachable_)(__builtin_expect(!!(current_code_reachable_), 1))) {
2574 if (!VALIDATE(TypeCheckReturn())) return 0;
2575 DoReturn();
2576 } else {
2577 // We pop all return values from the stack to check their type.
2578 // Since we deal with unreachable code, we do not have to keep the
2579 // values.
2580 int num_returns = static_cast<int>(this->sig_->return_count());
2581 for (int i = num_returns - 1; i >= 0; --i) {
2582 Pop(i, this->sig_->GetReturn(i));
2583 }
2584 }
2585
2586 EndControl();
2587 return 1;
2588 }
2589
2590 DECODE(Unreachable) {
2591 CALL_INTERFACE_IF_REACHABLE(Unreachable);
2592 EndControl();
2593 return 1;
2594 }
2595
2596 DECODE(I32Const) {
2597 ImmI32Immediate<validate> imm(this, this->pc_ + 1);
2598 Value* value = Push(kWasmI32);
2599 CALL_INTERFACE_IF_REACHABLE(I32Const, value, imm.value);
2600 return 1 + imm.length;
2601 }
2602

2605 Value* value = Push(kWasmI64);
2606 CALL_INTERFACE_IF_REACHABLE(I64Const, value, imm.value);
2607 return 1 + imm.length;
2608 }
2609

2613 CALL_INTERFACE_IF_REACHABLE(F32Const, value, imm.value);
2614 return 1 + imm.length;
2615 }
2616
2617 DECODE(F64Const) {
2618 ImmF64Immediate<validate> imm(this, this->pc_ + 1);

2620 CALL_INTERFACE_IF_REACHABLE(F64Const, value, imm.value);

2622 }
2623
2624 DECODE(RefNull) {
2625 CHECK_PROTOTYPE_OPCODE(reftypes);
2626 HeapTypeImmediate<validate> imm(this->enabled_, this, this->pc_ + 1);
2627 if (!this->Validate(this->pc_ + 1, imm)) return 0;
2628 Value* value = Push(ValueType::Ref(imm.type, kNullable));
2629 CALL_INTERFACE_IF_REACHABLE(RefNull, value);
2630 return 1 + imm.length;
2631 }
2632
2633 DECODE(RefIsNull) {
2634 CHECK_PROTOTYPE_OPCODE(reftypes);
2635 Value value = Pop(0);
2636 Value* result = Push(kWasmI32);
2637 switch (value.type.kind()) {
2638 case ValueType::kOptRef:
2639 CALL_INTERFACE_IF_REACHABLE(UnOp, kExprRefIsNull, value, result);
2640 return 1;
2641 case ValueType::kRef:
2642 // For non-nullable references, the result is always false.
2643 CALL_INTERFACE_IF_REACHABLE(I32Const, result, 0);
2644 return 1;
2645 default:
2646 if (validate) {
2647 this->errorf(this->pc_,
2648 "invalid argument type to ref.is_null. Expected "
2649 "reference type, got %s",
2650 value.type.name().c_str());
2651 return 0;
2652 }
2653 UNREACHABLE()V8_Fatal("unreachable code");
2654 }
2655 }
2656
2657 DECODE(RefFunc) {
2658 CHECK_PROTOTYPE_OPCODE(reftypes);
2659 FunctionIndexImmediate<validate> imm(this, this->pc_ + 1);
2660 if (!this->Validate(this->pc_ + 1, imm)) return 0;
2661 HeapType heap_type(this->enabled_.has_typed_funcref()
2662 ? this->module_->functions[imm.index].sig_index
2663 : HeapType::kFunc);
2664 Value* value = Push(ValueType::Ref(heap_type, kNonNullable));
2665 CALL_INTERFACE_IF_REACHABLE(RefFunc, imm.index, value);
2666 return 1 + imm.length;
2667 }
2668
2669 DECODE(RefAsNonNull) {
2670 CHECK_PROTOTYPE_OPCODE(typed_funcref);
2671 Value value = Pop(0);
2672 switch (value.type.kind()) {
2673 case ValueType::kRef: {
2674 Value* result = Push(value.type);
2675 CALL_INTERFACE_IF_REACHABLE(PassThrough, value, result);
2676 return 1;
2677 }
2678 case ValueType::kOptRef: {
2679 Value* result =
2680 Push(ValueType::Ref(value.type.heap_type(), kNonNullable));
2681 CALL_INTERFACE_IF_REACHABLE(RefAsNonNull, value, result);
2682 return 1;
2683 }
2684 default:
2685 if (validate) {
2686 this->errorf(this->pc_,
2687 "invalid agrument type to ref.as_non_null: Expected "
2688 "reference type, got %s",
2689 value.type.name().c_str());
2690 }
2691 return 0;
2692 }
2693 }
2694
2695 DECODE(LocalGet) {
2696 LocalIndexImmediate<validate> imm(this, this->pc_ + 1);
2697 if (!this->Validate(this->pc_ + 1, imm)) return 0;
2698 Value* value = Push(this->local_type(imm.index));
2699 CALL_INTERFACE_IF_REACHABLE(LocalGet, value, imm);
2700 return 1 + imm.length;
2701 }
2702
2703 DECODE(LocalSet) {
2704 LocalIndexImmediate<validate> imm(this, this->pc_ + 1);
2705 if (!this->Validate(this->pc_ + 1, imm)) return 0;
2706 Value value = Pop(0, this->local_type(imm.index));
2707 CALL_INTERFACE_IF_REACHABLE(LocalSet, value, imm);
2708 return 1 + imm.length;
2709 }
2710
2711 DECODE(LocalTee) {
2712 LocalIndexImmediate<validate> imm(this, this->pc_ + 1);
2713 if (!this->Validate(this->pc_ + 1, imm)) return 0;
2714 Value value = Pop(0, this->local_type(imm.index));
2715 Value* result = Push(value.type);
2716 CALL_INTERFACE_IF_REACHABLE(LocalTee, value, result, imm);
2717 return 1 + imm.length;
2718 }
2719
2720 DECODE(Drop) {
2721 Value value = Pop(0);
2722 CALL_INTERFACE_IF_REACHABLE(Drop, value);
2723 return 1;
2724 }
2725
2726 DECODE(GlobalGet) {
2727 GlobalIndexImmediate<validate> imm(this, this->pc_ + 1);
2728 if (!this->Validate(this->pc_ + 1, imm)) return 0;
2729 Value* result = Push(imm.type);
2730 CALL_INTERFACE_IF_REACHABLE(GlobalGet, result, imm);
2731 return 1 + imm.length;
2732 }
