2734 DECODE(GlobalSet) {
2735 GlobalIndexImmediate<validate> imm(this, this->pc_ + 1);
2736 if (!this->Validate(this->pc_ + 1, imm)) return 0;
2737 if (!VALIDATE(imm.global->mutability)) {
2738 this->errorf(this->pc_, "immutable global #%u cannot be assigned",
2739 imm.index);
2740 return 0;
2741 }
2742 Value value = Pop(0, imm.type);
2743 CALL_INTERFACE_IF_REACHABLE(GlobalSet, value, imm);
2744 return 1 + imm.length;
2745 }
2746
2747 DECODE(TableGet) {
2748 CHECK_PROTOTYPE_OPCODE(reftypes);
2749 TableIndexImmediate<validate> imm(this, this->pc_ + 1);
2750 if (!this->Validate(this->pc_ + 1, imm)) return 0;
2751 Value index = Pop(0, kWasmI32);
2752 Value* result = Push(this->module_->tables[imm.index].type);
2753 CALL_INTERFACE_IF_REACHABLE(TableGet, index, result, imm);
2754 return 1 + imm.length;
2755 }
2756
2757 DECODE(TableSet) {
2758 CHECK_PROTOTYPE_OPCODE(reftypes);
2759 TableIndexImmediate<validate> imm(this, this->pc_ + 1);
2760 if (!this->Validate(this->pc_ + 1, imm)) return 0;
2761 Value value = Pop(1, this->module_->tables[imm.index].type);
2762 Value index = Pop(0, kWasmI32);
2763 CALL_INTERFACE_IF_REACHABLE(TableSet, index, value, imm);
2764 return 1 + imm.length;
2765 }
2766
2767 DECODE(LoadMem) {
2768 // Hard-code the list of load types. The opcodes are highly unlikely to
2769 // ever change, and we have some checks here to guard against that.
2770 static_assert(sizeof(LoadType) == sizeof(uint8_t), "LoadType is compact");
2771 static constexpr uint8_t kMinOpcode = kExprI32LoadMem;
2772 static constexpr uint8_t kMaxOpcode = kExprI64LoadMem32U;
2773 static constexpr LoadType kLoadTypes[] = {
2774 LoadType::kI32Load, LoadType::kI64Load, LoadType::kF32Load,
2775 LoadType::kF64Load, LoadType::kI32Load8S, LoadType::kI32Load8U,
2776 LoadType::kI32Load16S, LoadType::kI32Load16U, LoadType::kI64Load8S,
2777 LoadType::kI64Load8U, LoadType::kI64Load16S, LoadType::kI64Load16U,
2778 LoadType::kI64Load32S, LoadType::kI64Load32U};
2779 STATIC_ASSERT(arraysize(kLoadTypes) == kMaxOpcode - kMinOpcode + 1)static_assert((sizeof(ArraySizeHelper(kLoadTypes))) == kMaxOpcode
- kMinOpcode + 1, "arraysize(kLoadTypes) == kMaxOpcode - kMinOpcode + 1"
);
2780 DCHECK_LE(kMinOpcode, opcode)((void) 0);
2781 DCHECK_GE(kMaxOpcode, opcode)((void) 0);
2782 return DecodeLoadMem(kLoadTypes[opcode - kMinOpcode]);
2783 }
2784
2785 DECODE(StoreMem) {
2786 // Hard-code the list of store types. The opcodes are highly unlikely to
2787 // ever change, and we have some checks here to guard against that.
2788 static_assert(sizeof(StoreType) == sizeof(uint8_t), "StoreType is compact");
2789 static constexpr uint8_t kMinOpcode = kExprI32StoreMem;
2790 static constexpr uint8_t kMaxOpcode = kExprI64StoreMem32;
2791 static constexpr StoreType kStoreTypes[] = {
2792 StoreType::kI32Store, StoreType::kI64Store, StoreType::kF32Store,
2793 StoreType::kF64Store, StoreType::kI32Store8, StoreType::kI32Store16,
2794 StoreType::kI64Store8, StoreType::kI64Store16, StoreType::kI64Store32};
2795 STATIC_ASSERT(arraysize(kStoreTypes) == kMaxOpcode - kMinOpcode + 1)static_assert((sizeof(ArraySizeHelper(kStoreTypes))) == kMaxOpcode
- kMinOpcode + 1, "arraysize(kStoreTypes) == kMaxOpcode - kMinOpcode + 1"
);
2796 DCHECK_LE(kMinOpcode, opcode)((void) 0);
2797 DCHECK_GE(kMaxOpcode, opcode)((void) 0);
2798 return DecodeStoreMem(kStoreTypes[opcode - kMinOpcode]);
2799 }

2802 if (!CheckHasMemory()) return 0;

2804 if (!VALIDATE(this->module_->origin == kWasmOrigin)) {
2805 this->error("grow_memory is not supported for asmjs modules");
2806 return 0;
2807 }
2808 Value value = Pop(0, kWasmI32);
2809 Value* result = Push(kWasmI32);
2810 CALL_INTERFACE_IF_REACHABLE(MemoryGrow, value, result);
2811 return 1 + imm.length;
2812 }

2827 CALL_INTERFACE_IF_REACHABLE(CallDirect, imm, args.begin(), returns);
2828 return 1 + imm.length;

2835 ArgVector args = PopArgs(imm.sig);
2836 Value* returns = PushReturns(imm.sig);
2837 CALL_INTERFACE_IF_REACHABLE(CallIndirect, index, imm, args.begin(),

2875 DECODE(CallRef) {
2876 CHECK_PROTOTYPE_OPCODE(typed_funcref);
2877 Value func_ref = Pop(0);
2878 ValueType func_type = func_ref.type;
2879 if (!func_type.is_object_reference_type() || !func_type.has_index() ||
2880 !this->module_->has_signature(func_type.ref_index())) {
2881 this->errorf(this->pc_,
2882 "call_ref: Expected function reference on top of stack, "
2883 "found %s of type %s instead",
2884 SafeOpcodeNameAt(func_ref.pc), func_type.name().c_str());
2885 return 0;
2886 }
2887 const FunctionSig* sig = this->module_->signature(func_type.ref_index());
2888 ArgVector args = PopArgs(sig);
2889 Value* returns = PushReturns(sig);
2890 CALL_INTERFACE_IF_REACHABLE(CallRef, func_ref, sig, func_type.ref_index(),
2891 args.begin(), returns);
2892 return 1;
2893 }
2894
2895 DECODE(ReturnCallRef) {
2896 CHECK_PROTOTYPE_OPCODE(typed_funcref);
2897 CHECK_PROTOTYPE_OPCODE(return_call);
2898 Value func_ref = Pop(0);
2899 ValueType func_type = func_ref.type;
2900 if (!func_type.is_object_reference_type() || !func_type.has_index() ||
2901 !this->module_->has_signature(func_type.ref_index())) {
2902 this->errorf(this->pc_,
2903 "return_call_ref: Expected function reference on top of "
2904 "found %s of type %s instead",
2905 SafeOpcodeNameAt(func_ref.pc), func_type.name().c_str());
2906 return 0;
2907 }
2908 const FunctionSig* sig = this->module_->signature(func_type.ref_index());
2909 ArgVector args = PopArgs(sig);
2910 CALL_INTERFACE_IF_REACHABLE(ReturnCallRef, func_ref, sig,
2911 func_type.ref_index(), args.begin());
2912 EndControl();
2913 return 1;
2914 }
2915
2916 DECODE(Numeric) {
2917 byte numeric_index =
2918 this->template read_u8<validate>(this->pc_ + 1, "numeric index");
2919 WasmOpcode full_opcode =
2920 static_cast<WasmOpcode>(kNumericPrefix << 8 | numeric_index);
2921 if (full_opcode == kExprTableGrow || full_opcode == kExprTableSize ||
2922 full_opcode == kExprTableFill) {
2923 CHECK_PROTOTYPE_OPCODE(reftypes);
2924 } else if (full_opcode >= kExprMemoryInit) {
2925 CHECK_PROTOTYPE_OPCODE(bulk_memory);
2926 }
2927 trace_msg->AppendOpcode(full_opcode);
2928 return DecodeNumericOpcode(full_opcode);
2929 }
2930
2931 DECODE(Simd) {
2932 CHECK_PROTOTYPE_OPCODE(simd);
2933 uint32_t opcode_length = 0;
2934 WasmOpcode full_opcode = this->template read_prefixed_opcode<validate>(
2935 this->pc_, &opcode_length);
2936 if (!VALIDATE(this->ok())) return 0;
2937 trace_msg->AppendOpcode(full_opcode);
2938 return DecodeSimdOpcode(full_opcode, 1 + opcode_length);
2939 }
2940
2941 DECODE(Atomic) {
2942 CHECK_PROTOTYPE_OPCODE(threads);
2943 byte atomic_index =
2944 this->template read_u8<validate>(this->pc_ + 1, "atomic index");
2945 WasmOpcode full_opcode =
2946 static_cast<WasmOpcode>(kAtomicPrefix << 8 | atomic_index);
2947 trace_msg->AppendOpcode(full_opcode);
2948 return DecodeAtomicOpcode(full_opcode);
2949 }
2950
2951 DECODE(GC) {
2952 CHECK_PROTOTYPE_OPCODE(gc);
2953 byte gc_index = this->template read_u8<validate>(this->pc_ + 1, "gc index");
2954 WasmOpcode full_opcode = static_cast<WasmOpcode>(kGCPrefix << 8 | gc_index);
2955 trace_msg->AppendOpcode(full_opcode);
2956 return DecodeGCOpcode(full_opcode);
2957 }
2958
2959#define SIMPLE_PROTOTYPE_CASE(name, opc, sig) \
2960 DECODE(name) { return BuildSimplePrototypeOperator(opcode); }
2961 FOREACH_SIMPLE_PROTOTYPE_OPCODE(SIMPLE_PROTOTYPE_CASE)SIMPLE_PROTOTYPE_CASE(RefEq, 0xd5, i_qq)
2962#undef SIMPLE_PROTOTYPE_CASE
2963
2964 DECODE(UnknownOrAsmJs) {
2965 // Deal with special asmjs opcodes.
2966 if (!VALIDATE(is_asmjs_module(this->module_))) {
2967 this->errorf(this->pc(), "Invalid opcode 0x%x", opcode);
2968 return 0;
2969 }
2970 const FunctionSig* sig = WasmOpcodes::AsmjsSignature(opcode);
2971 DCHECK_NOT_NULL(sig)((void) 0);
2972 return BuildSimpleOperator(opcode, sig);
2973 }
2974
2975#undef DECODE
2976
2977 using OpcodeHandler = int (*)(WasmFullDecoder*, WasmOpcode);
2978
2979 // Ideally we would use template specialization for the different opcodes, but
2980 // GCC does not allow to specialize templates in class scope
2981 // (https://gcc.gnu.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=85282), and specializing
2982 // outside the class is not allowed for non-specialized classes.
2983 // Hence just list all implementations explicitly here, which also gives more
2984 // freedom to use the same implementation for different opcodes.
2985#define DECODE_IMPL(opcode) DECODE_IMPL2(kExpr##opcode, opcode)
2986#define DECODE_IMPL2(opcode, name) \
2987 if (idx == opcode) return &WasmFullDecoder::Decode##name

3055
3056 OpcodeHandler GetOpcodeHandler(uint8_t opcode) {
3057 static constexpr std::array<OpcodeHandler, 256> kOpcodeHandlers =
3058 base::make_array<256>(GetOpcodeHandlerTableEntry);
3059 return kOpcodeHandlers[opcode];
3060 }
3061
3062 void DecodeFunctionBody() {
3063 TRACE("wasm-decode %p...%p (module+%u, %d bytes)\n", this->start(),
3064 this->end(), this->pc_offset(),
3065 static_cast<int>(this->end() - this->start()));
3066
3067 // Set up initial function block.
3068 {
3069 Control* c = PushControl(kControlBlock);
3070 InitMerge(&c->start_merge, 0, [](uint32_t) -> Value { UNREACHABLE()V8_Fatal("unreachable code"); });
3071 InitMerge(&c->end_merge,
3072 static_cast<uint32_t>(this->sig_->return_count()),
3073 [&](uint32_t i) {
3074 return Value{this->pc_, this->sig_->GetReturn(i)};
3075 });
3076 CALL_INTERFACE(StartFunctionBody, c);
3077 }
3078
3079 // Decode the function body.
3080 while (this->pc_ < this->end_) {
3081 uint8_t first_byte = *this->pc_;
3082 WasmOpcode opcode = static_cast<WasmOpcode>(first_byte);
3083 CALL_INTERFACE_IF_REACHABLE(NextInstruction, opcode);
3084 OpcodeHandler handler = GetOpcodeHandler(first_byte);
3085 int len = (*handler)(this, opcode);
3086 this->pc_ += len;
3087 }
3088
3089 if (!VALIDATE(this->pc_ == this->end_)) {
3090 this->error("Beyond end of code");
3091 }
3092 }
3093
3094 void EndControl() {
3095 DCHECK(!control_.empty())((void) 0);
3096 Control* current = &control_.back();
3097 stack_.erase(stack_.begin() + current->stack_depth, stack_.end());
3098 CALL_INTERFACE_IF_REACHABLE(EndControl, current);
3099 current->reachability = kUnreachable;
3100 current_code_reachable_ = false;
3101 }
3102
3103 template <typename func>
3104 void InitMerge(Merge<Value>* merge, uint32_t arity, func get_val) {
3105 merge->arity = arity;
3106 if (arity == 1) {
3107 merge->vals.first = get_val(0);
3108 } else if (arity > 1) {
3109 merge->vals.array = this->zone()->template NewArray<Value>(arity);
3110 for (uint32_t i = 0; i < arity; i++) {
3111 merge->vals.array[i] = get_val(i);
3112 }
3113 }
3114 }
3115
3116 void SetBlockType(Control* c, BlockTypeImmediate<validate>& imm,
3117 Value* args) {
3118 const byte* pc = this->pc_;
3119 InitMerge(&c->end_merge, imm.out_arity(), [pc, &imm](uint32_t i) {
3120 return Value{pc, imm.out_type(i)};
3121 });
3122 InitMerge(&c->start_merge, imm.in_arity(),
3123 [args](uint32_t i) { return args[i]; });
3124 }
3125
3126 // Pops arguments as required by signature.
3127 V8_INLINEinline __attribute__((always_inline)) ArgVector PopArgs(const FunctionSig* sig) {
3128 int count = sig ? static_cast<int>(sig->parameter_count()) : 0;
3129 ArgVector args(count);
3130 for (int i = count - 1; i >= 0; --i) {
3131 args[i] = Pop(i, sig->GetParam(i));
3132 }
3133 return args;
3134 }
3135
3136 V8_INLINEinline __attribute__((always_inline)) ArgVector PopArgs(const StructType* type) {
3137 int count = static_cast<int>(type->field_count());
3138 ArgVector args(count);
3139 for (int i = count - 1; i >= 0; i--) {
3140 args[i] = Pop(i, type->field(i).Unpacked());
3141 }
3142 return args;
3143 }
3144
3145 V8_INLINEinline __attribute__((always_inline)) ArgVector PopArgs(uint32_t base_index,
3146 Vector<ValueType> arg_types) {
3147 ArgVector args(arg_types.size());
3148 for (int i = static_cast<int>(arg_types.size()) - 1; i >= 0; i--) {
3149 args[i] = Pop(base_index + i, arg_types[i]);
3150 }
3151 return args;
3152 }
3153
3154 ValueType GetReturnType(const FunctionSig* sig) {
3155 DCHECK_GE(1, sig->return_count())((void) 0);
3156 return sig->return_count() == 0 ? kWasmStmt : sig->GetReturn();
3157 }
3158
3159 Control* PushControl(ControlKind kind, uint32_t locals_count = 0) {
3160 Reachability reachability =
3161 control_.empty() ? kReachable : control_.back().innerReachability();
3162 control_.emplace_back(kind, locals_count, stack_size(), this->pc_,
3163 reachability);
3164 current_code_reachable_ = this->ok() && reachability == kReachable;
3165 return &control_.back();
3166 }
3167
3168 void PopControl(Control* c) {
3169 DCHECK_EQ(c, &control_.back())((void) 0);
3170 CALL_INTERFACE_IF_PARENT_REACHABLE(PopControl, c);
3171
3172 // A loop just leaves the values on the stack.
3173 if (!c->is_loop()) PushMergeValues(c, &c->end_merge);
3174
3175 bool parent_reached =
3176 c->reachable() || c->end_merge.reached || c->is_onearmed_if();
3177 control_.pop_back();
3178 // If the parent block was reachable before, but the popped control does not
3179 // return to here, this block becomes "spec only reachable".
3180 if (!parent_reached) SetSucceedingCodeDynamicallyUnreachable();
3181 current_code_reachable_ = control_.back().reachable();
3182 }
3183
3184 int DecodeLoadMem(LoadType type, int prefix_len = 1) {
3185 if (!CheckHasMemory()) return 0;
3186 MemoryAccessImmediate<validate> imm(this, this->pc_ + prefix_len,
3187 type.size_log_2());
3188 Value index = Pop(0, kWasmI32);
3189 Value* result = Push(type.value_type());
3190 CALL_INTERFACE_IF_REACHABLE(LoadMem, type, imm, index, result);
3191 return prefix_len + imm.length;
3192 }
3193
3194 int DecodeLoadTransformMem(LoadType type, LoadTransformationKind transform,
3195 uint32_t opcode_length) {
3196 if (!CheckHasMemory()) return 0;
3197 // Load extends always load 64-bits.
3198 uint32_t max_alignment =
3199 transform == LoadTransformationKind::kExtend ? 3 : type.size_log_2();
3200 MemoryAccessImmediate<validate> imm(this, this->pc_ + opcode_length,
3201 max_alignment);
3202 Value index = Pop(0, kWasmI32);
3203 Value* result = Push(kWasmS128);
3204 CALL_INTERFACE_IF_REACHABLE(LoadTransform, type, transform, imm, index,
3205 result);
3206 return opcode_length + imm.length;
3207 }
3208
3209 int DecodeStoreMem(StoreType store, int prefix_len = 1) {
3210 if (!CheckHasMemory()) return 0;
3211 MemoryAccessImmediate<validate> imm(this, this->pc_ + prefix_len,
3212 store.size_log_2());
3213 Value value = Pop(1, store.value_type());
3214 Value index = Pop(0, kWasmI32);
3215 CALL_INTERFACE_IF_REACHABLE(StoreMem, store, imm, index, value);
3216 return prefix_len + imm.length;
3217 }
3218
3219 bool ValidateBrTableTarget(uint32_t target, const byte* pos, int index) {
3220 if (!VALIDATE(target < this->control_.size())) {
3221 this->errorf(pos, "improper branch in br_table target %u (depth %u)",
3222 index, target);
3223 return false;
3224 }
3225 return true;
3226 }
3227
3228 std::vector<ValueType> InitializeBrTableResultTypes(uint32_t target) {
3229 Merge<Value>* merge = control_at(target)->br_merge();
3230 int br_arity = merge->arity;
3231 std::vector<ValueType> result(br_arity);
3232 for (int i = 0; i < br_arity; ++i) {
3233 result[i] = (*merge)[i].type;
3234 }
3235 return result;
3236 }
3237
3238 bool UpdateBrTableResultTypes(std::vector<ValueType>* result_types,
3239 uint32_t target, const byte* pos, int index) {
3240 Merge<Value>* merge = control_at(target)->br_merge();
3241 int br_arity = merge->arity;
3242 // First we check if the arities match.
3243 if (!VALIDATE(br_arity == static_cast<int>(result_types->size()))) {
3244 this->errorf(pos,
3245 "inconsistent arity in br_table target %u (previous was "
3246 "%zu, this one is %u)",
3247 index, result_types->size(), br_arity);
3248 return false;
3249 }
3250
3251 for (int i = 0; i < br_arity; ++i) {
3252 if (this->enabled_.has_reftypes()) {
3253 // The expected type is the biggest common sub type of all targets.
3254 ValueType type = (*result_types)[i];
3255 (*result_types)[i] =
3256 CommonSubtype((*result_types)[i], (*merge)[i].type, this->module_);
3257 if (!VALIDATE((*result_types)[i] != kWasmBottom)) {
3258 this->errorf(pos,
3259 "inconsistent type in br_table target %u (previous "
3260 "was %s, this one is %s)",
3261 index, type.name().c_str(),
3262 (*merge)[i].type.name().c_str());
3263 return false;
3264 }
3265 } else {
3266 // All target must have the same signature.
3267 if (!VALIDATE((*result_types)[i] == (*merge)[i].type)) {
3268 this->errorf(pos,
3269 "inconsistent type in br_table target %u (previous "
3270 "was %s, this one is %s)",
3271 index, (*result_types)[i].name().c_str(),
3272 (*merge)[i].type.name().c_str());
3273 return false;
3274 }
3275 }
3276 }
3277 return true;
3278 }
3279
3280 bool TypeCheckBrTable(const std::vector<ValueType>& result_types) {
3281 int br_arity = static_cast<int>(result_types.size());
3282 if (V8_LIKELY(!control_.back().unreachable())(__builtin_expect(!!(!control_.back().unreachable()), 1))) {
3283 int available =
3284 static_cast<int>(stack_.size()) - control_.back().stack_depth;
3285 // There have to be enough values on the stack.
3286 if (!VALIDATE(available >= br_arity)) {
3287 this->errorf(this->pc_,
3288 "expected %u elements on the stack for branch to "
3289 "@%d, found %u",
3290 br_arity, startrel(control_.back().pc), available);
3291 return false;
3292 }
3293 Value* stack_values = &*(stack_.end() - br_arity);
3294 // Type-check the topmost br_arity values on the stack.
3295 for (int i = 0; i < br_arity; ++i) {
3296 Value& val = stack_values[i];
3297 if (!VALIDATE(IsSubtypeOf(val.type, result_types[i], this->module_))) {
3298 this->errorf(this->pc_,
3299 "type error in merge[%u] (expected %s, got %s)", i,
3300 result_types[i].name().c_str(), val.type.name().c_str());
3301 return false;
3302 }
3303 }
3304 } else { // !control_.back().reachable()
3305 // Pop values from the stack, accoring to the expected signature.
3306 for (int i = 0; i < br_arity; ++i) Pop(i + 1, result_types[i]);
3307 }
3308 return this->ok();
3309 }
3310
3311 uint32_t SimdConstOp(uint32_t opcode_length) {
3312 Simd128Immediate<validate> imm(this, this->pc_ + opcode_length);
3313 auto* result = Push(kWasmS128);
3314 CALL_INTERFACE_IF_REACHABLE(S128Const, imm, result);
3315 return opcode_length + kSimd128Size;
3316 }
3317
3318 uint32_t SimdExtractLane(WasmOpcode opcode, ValueType type,
3319 uint32_t opcode_length) {
3320 SimdLaneImmediate<validate> imm(this, this->pc_ + opcode_length);
3321 if (this->Validate(this->pc_ + opcode_length, opcode, imm)) {
3322 Value inputs[] = {Pop(0, kWasmS128)};
3323 Value* result = Push(type);
3324 CALL_INTERFACE_IF_REACHABLE(SimdLaneOp, opcode, imm, ArrayVector(inputs),
3325 result);
3326 }
3327 return opcode_length + imm.length;
3328 }
3329
3330 uint32_t SimdReplaceLane(WasmOpcode opcode, ValueType type,
3331 uint32_t opcode_length) {
3332 SimdLaneImmediate<validate> imm(this, this->pc_ + opcode_length);
3333 if (this->Validate(this->pc_ + opcode_length, opcode, imm)) {
3334 Value inputs[2] = {UnreachableValue(this->pc_),
3335 UnreachableValue(this->pc_)};
3336 inputs[1] = Pop(1, type);
3337 inputs[0] = Pop(0, kWasmS128);
3338 Value* result = Push(kWasmS128);
3339 CALL_INTERFACE_IF_REACHABLE(SimdLaneOp, opcode, imm, ArrayVector(inputs),
3340 result);
3341 }
3342 return opcode_length + imm.length;
3343 }
3344
3345 uint32_t Simd8x16ShuffleOp(uint32_t opcode_length) {
3346 Simd128Immediate<validate> imm(this, this->pc_ + opcode_length);
3347 if (this->Validate(this->pc_ + opcode_length, imm)) {
3348 Value input1 = Pop(1, kWasmS128);
3349 Value input0 = Pop(0, kWasmS128);
3350 Value* result = Push(kWasmS128);
3351 CALL_INTERFACE_IF_REACHABLE(Simd8x16ShuffleOp, imm, input0, input1,
3352 result);
3353 }
3354 return opcode_length + 16;
3355 }
3356
3357 uint32_t DecodeSimdOpcode(WasmOpcode opcode, uint32_t opcode_length) {
3358 // opcode_length is the number of bytes that this SIMD-specific opcode takes
3359 // up in the LEB128 encoded form.
3360 switch (opcode) {
3361 case kExprF64x2ExtractLane:
3362 return SimdExtractLane(opcode, kWasmF64, opcode_length);
3363 case kExprF32x4ExtractLane:
3364 return SimdExtractLane(opcode, kWasmF32, opcode_length);
3365 case kExprI64x2ExtractLane:
3366 return SimdExtractLane(opcode, kWasmI64, opcode_length);
3367 case kExprI32x4ExtractLane:
3368 case kExprI16x8ExtractLaneS:
3369 case kExprI16x8ExtractLaneU:
3370 case kExprI8x16ExtractLaneS:
3371 case kExprI8x16ExtractLaneU:
3372 return SimdExtractLane(opcode, kWasmI32, opcode_length);
3373 case kExprF64x2ReplaceLane:
3374 return SimdReplaceLane(opcode, kWasmF64, opcode_length);
3375 case kExprF32x4ReplaceLane:
3376 return SimdReplaceLane(opcode, kWasmF32, opcode_length);
3377 case kExprI64x2ReplaceLane:
3378 return SimdReplaceLane(opcode, kWasmI64, opcode_length);
3379 case kExprI32x4ReplaceLane:
3380 case kExprI16x8ReplaceLane:
3381 case kExprI8x16ReplaceLane:
3382 return SimdReplaceLane(opcode, kWasmI32, opcode_length);
3383 case kExprS8x16Shuffle:
3384 return Simd8x16ShuffleOp(opcode_length);
3385 case kExprS128LoadMem:
3386 return DecodeLoadMem(LoadType::kS128Load, opcode_length);
3387 case kExprS128StoreMem:
3388 return DecodeStoreMem(StoreType::kS128Store, opcode_length);
3389 case kExprS128LoadMem32Zero:
3390 if (!CheckSimdPostMvp(opcode)) {
3391 return 0;
3392 }
3393 return DecodeLoadTransformMem(LoadType::kI32Load,
3394 LoadTransformationKind::kZeroExtend,
3395 opcode_length);
3396 case kExprS128LoadMem64Zero:
3397 if (!CheckSimdPostMvp(opcode)) {
3398 return 0;
3399 }
3400 return DecodeLoadTransformMem(LoadType::kI64Load,
3401 LoadTransformationKind::kZeroExtend,
3402 opcode_length);
3403 case kExprS8x16LoadSplat:
3404 return DecodeLoadTransformMem(LoadType::kI32Load8S,
3405 LoadTransformationKind::kSplat,
3406 opcode_length);
3407 case kExprS16x8LoadSplat:
3408 return DecodeLoadTransformMem(LoadType::kI32Load16S,
3409 LoadTransformationKind::kSplat,
3410 opcode_length);
3411 case kExprS32x4LoadSplat:
3412 return DecodeLoadTransformMem(
3413 LoadType::kI32Load, LoadTransformationKind::kSplat, opcode_length);
3414 case kExprS64x2LoadSplat:
3415 return DecodeLoadTransformMem(
3416 LoadType::kI64Load, LoadTransformationKind::kSplat, opcode_length);
3417 case kExprI16x8Load8x8S:
3418 return DecodeLoadTransformMem(LoadType::kI32Load8S,
3419 LoadTransformationKind::kExtend,
3420 opcode_length);
3421 case kExprI16x8Load8x8U:
3422 return DecodeLoadTransformMem(LoadType::kI32Load8U,
3423 LoadTransformationKind::kExtend,
3424 opcode_length);
3425 case kExprI32x4Load16x4S:
3426 return DecodeLoadTransformMem(LoadType::kI32Load16S,
3427 LoadTransformationKind::kExtend,
3428 opcode_length);
3429 case kExprI32x4Load16x4U:
3430 return DecodeLoadTransformMem(LoadType::kI32Load16U,
3431 LoadTransformationKind::kExtend,
3432 opcode_length);
3433 case kExprI64x2Load32x2S:
3434 return DecodeLoadTransformMem(LoadType::kI64Load32S,
3435 LoadTransformationKind::kExtend,
3436 opcode_length);
3437 case kExprI64x2Load32x2U:
3438 return DecodeLoadTransformMem(LoadType::kI64Load32U,
3439 LoadTransformationKind::kExtend,
3440 opcode_length);
3441 case kExprS128Const:
3442 return SimdConstOp(opcode_length);
3443 default: {
3444 if (!CheckSimdPostMvp(opcode)) {
3445 return 0;
3446 }
3447 const FunctionSig* sig = WasmOpcodes::Signature(opcode);
3448 if (!VALIDATE(sig != nullptr)) {
3449 this->error("invalid simd opcode");
3450 return 0;
3451 }
3452 ArgVector args = PopArgs(sig);
3453 Value* results =
3454 sig->return_count() == 0 ? nullptr : Push(GetReturnType(sig));
3455 CALL_INTERFACE_IF_REACHABLE(SimdOp, opcode, VectorOf(args), results);
3456 return opcode_length;
3457 }
3458 }
3459 }
3460
3461 int DecodeGCOpcode(WasmOpcode opcode) {
3462 switch (opcode) {
3463 case kExprStructNewWithRtt: {
3464 StructIndexImmediate<validate> imm(this, this->pc_ + 2);
3465 if (!this->Validate(this->pc_ + 2, imm)) return 0;
3466 Value rtt = Pop(imm.struct_type->field_count());
3467 if (!VALIDATE(rtt.type.kind() == ValueType::kRtt)) {
3468 this->errorf(this->pc_,
3469 "struct.new_with_rtt expected rtt, found %s of type %s",
3470 SafeOpcodeNameAt(rtt.pc), rtt.type.name().c_str());
3471 return 0;
3472 }
3473 // TODO(7748): Drop this check if {imm} is dropped from the proposal
3474 // à la https://github.com/WebAssembly/function-references/pull/31.
3475 if (!VALIDATE(rtt.type.heap_representation() == imm.index)) {
3476 this->errorf(this->pc_,
3477 "struct.new_with_rtt expected rtt for type %d, found "
3478 "rtt for type %s",
3479 imm.index, rtt.type.heap_type().name().c_str());
3480 return 0;
3481 }
3482 ArgVector args = PopArgs(imm.struct_type);
3483 Value* value = Push(ValueType::Ref(imm.index, kNonNullable));
3484 CALL_INTERFACE_IF_REACHABLE(StructNewWithRtt, imm, rtt, args.begin(),
3485 value);
3486 return 2 + imm.length;
3487 }
3488 case kExprStructNewDefault: {
3489 StructIndexImmediate<validate> imm(this, this->pc_ + 2);
3490 if (!this->Validate(this->pc_ + 2, imm)) return 0;
3491 if (validate) {
3492 for (uint32_t i = 0; i < imm.struct_type->field_count(); i++) {
3493 ValueType ftype = imm.struct_type->field(i);
3494 if (!VALIDATE(ftype.is_defaultable())) {
3495 this->errorf(this->pc_,
3496 "struct.new_default_with_rtt: struct type %d has "
3497 "non-defaultable type %s for field %d",
3498 imm.index, ftype.name().c_str(), i);
3499 return 0;
3500 }
3501 }
3502 }
3503 Value rtt = Pop(0);
3504 if (!VALIDATE(rtt.type.kind() == ValueType::kRtt)) {
3505 this->errorf(
3506 this->pc_,
3507 "struct.new_default_with_rtt expected rtt, found %s of type %s",
3508 SafeOpcodeNameAt(rtt.pc), rtt.type.name().c_str());
3509 return 0;
3510 }
3511 // TODO(7748): Drop this check if {imm} is dropped from the proposal
3512 // à la https://github.com/WebAssembly/function-references/pull/31.
3513 if (!VALIDATE(rtt.type.heap_representation() == imm.index)) {
3514 this->errorf(
3515 this->pc_,
3516 "struct.new_default_with_rtt expected rtt for type %d, found "
3517 "rtt for type %s",
3518 imm.index, rtt.type.heap_type().name().c_str());
3519 return 0;
3520 }
3521 Value* value = Push(ValueType::Ref(imm.index, kNonNullable));
3522 CALL_INTERFACE_IF_REACHABLE(StructNewDefault, imm, rtt, value);
3523 return 2 + imm.length;
3524 }
3525 case kExprStructGet: {
3526 FieldIndexImmediate<validate> field(this, this->pc_ + 2);
3527 if (!this->Validate(this->pc_ + 2, field)) return 0;
3528 ValueType field_type =
3529 field.struct_index.struct_type->field(field.index);
3530 if (!VALIDATE(!field_type.is_packed())) {
3531 this->error(this->pc_,
3532 "struct.get used with a field of packed type. "
3533 "Use struct.get_s or struct.get_u instead.");
3534 return 0;
3535 }
3536 Value struct_obj =
3537 Pop(0, ValueType::Ref(field.struct_index.index, kNullable));
3538 Value* value = Push(field_type);
3539 CALL_INTERFACE_IF_REACHABLE(StructGet, struct_obj, field, true, value);
3540 return 2 + field.length;
3541 }
3542 case kExprStructGetU:
3543 case kExprStructGetS: {
3544 FieldIndexImmediate<validate> field(this, this->pc_ + 2);
3545 if (!this->Validate(this->pc_ + 2, field)) return 0;
3546 ValueType field_type =
3547 field.struct_index.struct_type->field(field.index);
3548 if (!VALIDATE(field_type.is_packed())) {
3549 this->errorf(this->pc_,
3550 "%s is only valid for packed struct fields. "
3551 "Use struct.get instead.",
3552 WasmOpcodes::OpcodeName(opcode));
3553 return 0;
3554 }
3555 Value struct_obj =
3556 Pop(0, ValueType::Ref(field.struct_index.index, kNullable));
3557 Value* value = Push(field_type.Unpacked());
3558 CALL_INTERFACE_IF_REACHABLE(StructGet, struct_obj, field,
3559 opcode == kExprStructGetS, value);
3560 return 2 + field.length;
3561 }
3562 case kExprStructSet: {
3563 FieldIndexImmediate<validate> field(this, this->pc_ + 2);
3564 if (!this->Validate(this->pc_ + 2, field)) return 0;
3565 const StructType* struct_type = field.struct_index.struct_type;
3566 if (!VALIDATE(struct_type->mutability(field.index))) {
3567 this->error(this->pc_, "setting immutable struct field");
3568 return 0;
3569 }
3570 Value field_value = Pop(1, struct_type->field(field.index).Unpacked());
3571 Value struct_obj =
3572 Pop(0, ValueType::Ref(field.struct_index.index, kNullable));
3573 CALL_INTERFACE_IF_REACHABLE(StructSet, struct_obj, field, field_value);
3574 return 2 + field.length;
3575 }
3576 case kExprArrayNewWithRtt: {
3577 ArrayIndexImmediate<validate> imm(this, this->pc_ + 2);
3578 if (!this->Validate(this->pc_ + 2, imm)) return 0;
3579 Value rtt = Pop(2);
3580 if (!VALIDATE(rtt.type.kind() == ValueType::kRtt)) {
3581 this->errorf(this->pc_ + 2,
3582 "array.new_with_rtt expected rtt, found %s of type %s",
3583 SafeOpcodeNameAt(rtt.pc), rtt.type.name().c_str());
3584 return 0;
3585 }
3586 // TODO(7748): Drop this check if {imm} is dropped from the proposal
3587 // à la https://github.com/WebAssembly/function-references/pull/31.
3588 if (!VALIDATE(rtt.type.heap_representation() == imm.index)) {
3589 this->errorf(this->pc_ + 2,
3590 "array.new_with_rtt expected rtt for type %d, found "
3591 "rtt for type %s",
3592 imm.index, rtt.type.heap_type().name().c_str());
3593 return 0;
3594 }
3595 Value length = Pop(1, kWasmI32);
3596 Value initial_value = Pop(0, imm.array_type->element_type().Unpacked());
3597 Value* value = Push(ValueType::Ref(imm.index, kNonNullable));
3598 CALL_INTERFACE_IF_REACHABLE(ArrayNewWithRtt, imm, length, initial_value,
3599 rtt, value);
3600 return 2 + imm.length;
3601 }
3602 case kExprArrayNewDefault: {
3603 ArrayIndexImmediate<validate> imm(this, this->pc_ + 2);
3604 if (!this->Validate(this->pc_ + 2, imm)) return 0;
3605 if (!VALIDATE(imm.array_type->element_type().is_defaultable())) {
3606 this->errorf(this->pc_,
3607 "array.new_default_with_rtt: array type %d has "
3608 "non-defaultable element type %s",
3609 imm.index,
3610 imm.array_type->element_type().name().c_str());
3611 return 0;
3612 }
3613 Value rtt = Pop(1);
3614 if (!VALIDATE(rtt.type.kind() == ValueType::kRtt)) {
3615 this->errorf(
3616 this->pc_ + 2,
3617 "array.new_default_with_rtt expected rtt, found %s of type %s",
3618 SafeOpcodeNameAt(rtt.pc), rtt.type.name().c_str());
3619 return 0;
3620 }
3621 // TODO(7748): Drop this check if {imm} is dropped from the proposal
3622 // à la https://github.com/WebAssembly/function-references/pull/31.
3623 if (!VALIDATE(rtt.type.heap_representation() == imm.index)) {
3624 this->errorf(this->pc_ + 2,
3625 "array.new_default_with_rtt expected rtt for type %d, "
3626 "found rtt for type %s",
3627 imm.index, rtt.type.heap_type().name().c_str());
3628 return 0;
3629 }
3630 Value length = Pop(0, kWasmI32);
3631 Value* value = Push(ValueType::Ref(imm.index, kNonNullable));
3632 CALL_INTERFACE_IF_REACHABLE(ArrayNewDefault, imm, length, rtt, value);
3633 return 2 + imm.length;
3634 }
3635 case kExprArrayGetS:
3636 case kExprArrayGetU: {
3637 ArrayIndexImmediate<validate> imm(this, this->pc_ + 2);
3638 if (!this->Validate(this->pc_ + 2, imm)) return 0;
3639 if (!VALIDATE(imm.array_type->element_type().is_packed())) {
3640 this->errorf(
3641 this->pc_,
3642 "%s is only valid for packed arrays. Use array.get instead.",
3643 WasmOpcodes::OpcodeName(opcode));
3644 return 0;
3645 }
3646 Value index = Pop(1, kWasmI32);
3647 Value array_obj = Pop(0, ValueType::Ref(imm.index, kNullable));
3648 Value* value = Push(imm.array_type->element_type().Unpacked());
3649 CALL_INTERFACE_IF_REACHABLE(ArrayGet, array_obj, imm, index,
3650 opcode == kExprArrayGetS, value);
3651 return 2 + imm.length;
3652 }
3653 case kExprArrayGet: {
3654 ArrayIndexImmediate<validate> imm(this, this->pc_ + 2);
3655 if (!this->Validate(this->pc_ + 2, imm)) return 0;
3656 if (!VALIDATE(!imm.array_type->element_type().is_packed())) {
3657 this->error(this->pc_,
3658 "array.get used with a field of packed type. "
3659 "Use array.get_s or array.get_u instead.");
3660 return 0;
3661 }
3662 Value index = Pop(1, kWasmI32);
3663 Value array_obj = Pop(0, ValueType::Ref(imm.index, kNullable));
3664 Value* value = Push(imm.array_type->element_type());
3665 CALL_INTERFACE_IF_REACHABLE(ArrayGet, array_obj, imm, index, true,
3666 value);
3667 return 2 + imm.length;
3668 }
3669 case kExprArraySet: {
3670 ArrayIndexImmediate<validate> imm(this, this->pc_ + 2);
3671 if (!this->Validate(this->pc_ + 2, imm)) return 0;
3672 if (!VALIDATE(imm.array_type->mutability())) {
3673 this->error(this->pc_, "setting element of immutable array");
3674 return 0;
3675 }
3676 Value value = Pop(2, imm.array_type->element_type().Unpacked());
3677 Value index = Pop(1, kWasmI32);
3678 Value array_obj = Pop(0, ValueType::Ref(imm.index, kNullable));
3679 CALL_INTERFACE_IF_REACHABLE(ArraySet, array_obj, imm, index, value);
3680 return 2 + imm.length;
3681 }
3682 case kExprArrayLen: {
3683 ArrayIndexImmediate<validate> imm(this, this->pc_ + 2);
3684 if (!this->Validate(this->pc_ + 2, imm)) return 0;
3685 Value array_obj = Pop(0, ValueType::Ref(imm.index, kNullable));
3686 Value* value = Push(kWasmI32);
3687 CALL_INTERFACE_IF_REACHABLE(ArrayLen, array_obj, value);
3688 return 2 + imm.length;
3689 }
3690 case kExprI31New: {
3691 Value input = Pop(0, kWasmI32);
3692 Value* value = Push(kWasmI31Ref);
3693 CALL_INTERFACE_IF_REACHABLE(I31New, input, value);
3694 return 2;
3695 }
3696 case kExprI31GetS: {
3697 Value i31 = Pop(0, kWasmI31Ref);
3698 Value* value = Push(kWasmI32);
3699 CALL_INTERFACE_IF_REACHABLE(I31GetS, i31, value);
3700 return 2;
3701 }
3702 case kExprI31GetU: {
3703 Value i31 = Pop(0, kWasmI31Ref);
3704 Value* value = Push(kWasmI32);
3705 CALL_INTERFACE_IF_REACHABLE(I31GetU, i31, value);
3706 return 2;
3707 }
3708 case kExprRttCanon: {
3709 HeapTypeImmediate<validate> imm(this->enabled_, this, this->pc_ + 2);
3710 if (!this->Validate(this->pc_ + 2, imm)) return 0;
3711 Value* value = Push(ValueType::Rtt(imm.type, 1));
3712 CALL_INTERFACE_IF_REACHABLE(RttCanon, imm, value);
3713 return 2 + imm.length;
3714 }
3715 case kExprRttSub: {
3716 // TODO(7748): The proposal currently includes additional immediates
3717 // here: the subtyping depth <n> and the "parent type", see:
3718 // https://github.com/WebAssembly/gc/commit/20a80e34 .
3719 // If these immediates don't get dropped (in the spirit of
3720 // https://github.com/WebAssembly/function-references/pull/31 ),
3721 // implement them here.
3722 HeapTypeImmediate<validate> imm(this->enabled_, this, this->pc_ + 2);
3723 if (!this->Validate(this->pc_ + 2, imm)) return 0;
3724 Value parent = Pop(0);
3725 // TODO(7748): Consider exposing "IsSubtypeOfHeap(HeapType t1, t2)" so
3726 // we can avoid creating (ref heaptype) wrappers here.
3727 if (!VALIDATE(parent.type.kind() == ValueType::kRtt &&
3728 IsSubtypeOf(
3729 ValueType::Ref(imm.type, kNonNullable),
3730 ValueType::Ref(parent.type.heap_type(), kNonNullable),
3731 this->module_))) {
3732 this->error(this->pc_, "rtt.sub requires a supertype rtt on stack");
3733 return 0;
3734 }
3735 Value* value = Push(ValueType::Rtt(imm.type, parent.type.depth() + 1));
3736 CALL_INTERFACE_IF_REACHABLE(RttSub, imm, parent, value);
3737 return 2 + imm.length;
3738 }
3739 case kExprRefTest: {
3740 // "Tests whether {obj}'s runtime type is a runtime subtype of {rtt}."
3741 HeapTypeImmediate<validate> obj_type(this->enabled_, this,
3742 this->pc_ + 2);
3743 if (!this->Validate(this->pc_ + 2, obj_type)) return 0;
3744 int len = 2 + obj_type.length;
3745 HeapTypeImmediate<validate> rtt_type(this->enabled_, this,
3746 this->pc_ + len);
3747 if (!this->Validate(this->pc_ + len, rtt_type)) return 0;
3748 len += rtt_type.length;
3749 // The static type of {obj} must be a supertype of the {rtt}'s type.
3750 if (!VALIDATE(IsSubtypeOf(ValueType::Ref(rtt_type.type, kNonNullable),
3751 ValueType::Ref(obj_type.type, kNonNullable),
3752 this->module_))) {
3753 this->errorf(this->pc_,
3754 "ref.test: rtt type must be subtype of object type");
3755 return 0;
3756 }
3757 Value rtt = Pop(1);
3758 if (!VALIDATE(rtt.type.kind() == ValueType::kRtt &&
3759 rtt.type.heap_type() == rtt_type.type)) {
3760 this->errorf(this->pc_,
3761 "ref.test: expected rtt for type %s but got %s",
3762 rtt_type.type.name().c_str(), rtt.type.name().c_str());
3763 return 0;
3764 }
3765 Value obj = Pop(0, ValueType::Ref(obj_type.type, kNullable));
3766 Value* value = Push(kWasmI32);
3767 CALL_INTERFACE_IF_REACHABLE(RefTest, obj, rtt, value);
3768 return len;
3769 }
3770 case kExprRefCast: {
3771 HeapTypeImmediate<validate> obj_type(this->enabled_, this,
3772 this->pc_ + 2);
3773 if (!this->Validate(this->pc_ + 2, obj_type)) return 0;
3774 int len = 2 + obj_type.length;
3775 HeapTypeImmediate<validate> rtt_type(this->enabled_, this,
3776 this->pc_ + len);
3777 if (!this->Validate(this->pc_ + len, rtt_type)) return 0;
3778 len += rtt_type.length;
3779 if (!VALIDATE(IsSubtypeOf(ValueType::Ref(rtt_type.type, kNonNullable),
3780 ValueType::Ref(obj_type.type, kNonNullable),
3781 this->module_))) {
3782 this->errorf(this->pc_,
3783 "ref.cast: rtt type must be subtype of object type");
3784 return 0;
3785 }
3786 Value rtt = Pop(1);
3787 if (!VALIDATE(rtt.type.kind() == ValueType::kRtt &&
3788 rtt.type.heap_type() == rtt_type.type)) {
3789 this->errorf(this->pc_,
3790 "ref.cast: expected rtt for type %s but got %s",
3791 rtt_type.type.name().c_str(), rtt.type.name().c_str());
3792 return 0;
3793 }
3794 Value obj = Pop(0, ValueType::Ref(obj_type.type, kNullable));
3795 Value* value = Push(ValueType::Ref(rtt_type.type, kNonNullable));
3796 CALL_INTERFACE_IF_REACHABLE(RefCast, obj, rtt, value);
3797 return len;
3798 }
3799 case kExprBrOnCast: {
3800 BranchDepthImmediate<validate> branch_depth(this, this->pc_ + 2);
3801 if (!this->Validate(this->pc_ + 2, branch_depth, control_.size())) {
3802 return 0;
3803 }
3804 // TODO(7748): If the heap type immediates remain in the spec, read
3805 // them here.
3806 Value rtt = Pop(1);
3807 if (!VALIDATE(rtt.type.kind() == ValueType::kRtt)) {
3808 this->error(this->pc_, "br_on_cast[1]: expected rtt on stack");
3809 return 0;
3810 }
3811 Value obj = Pop(0);
3812 if (!VALIDATE(obj.type.is_object_reference_type())) {
3813 this->error(this->pc_, "br_on_cast[0]: expected reference on stack");
3814 return 0;
3815 }
3816 // The static type of {obj} must be a supertype of {rtt}'s type.
3817 if (!VALIDATE(
3818 IsSubtypeOf(ValueType::Ref(rtt.type.heap_type(), kNonNullable),
3819 ValueType::Ref(obj.type.heap_type(), kNonNullable),
3820 this->module_))) {
3821 this->error(this->pc_,
3822 "br_on_cast: rtt type must be a subtype of object type");
3823 return 0;
3824 }
3825 Control* c = control_at(branch_depth.depth);
3826 Value* result_on_branch =
3827 Push(ValueType::Ref(rtt.type.heap_type(), kNonNullable));
3828 TypeCheckBranchResult check_result = TypeCheckBranch(c, true);
3829 if (V8_LIKELY(check_result == kReachableBranch)(__builtin_expect(!!(check_result == kReachableBranch), 1))) {
3830 CALL_INTERFACE(BrOnCast, obj, rtt, result_on_branch,
3831 branch_depth.depth);
3832 c->br_merge()->reached = true;
3833 } else if (check_result == kInvalidStack) {
3834 return 0;
3835 }
3836 Pop(0); // Drop {result_on_branch}, restore original value.
3837 Value* result_on_fallthrough = Push(obj.type);
3838 *result_on_fallthrough = obj;
3839 return 2 + branch_depth.length;
3840 }
3841 default:
3842 this->error("invalid gc opcode");
3843 return 0;
3844 }
3845 }
3846
3847 uint32_t DecodeAtomicOpcode(WasmOpcode opcode) {
3848 ValueType ret_type;
3849 const FunctionSig* sig = WasmOpcodes::Signature(opcode);
3850 if (!VALIDATE(sig != nullptr)) {
3851 this->error("invalid atomic opcode");
3852 return 0;
3853 }
3854 MachineType memtype;
3855 switch (opcode) {
3856#define CASE_ATOMIC_STORE_OP(Name, Type)case kExprName: { memtype = MachineType::Type(); ret_type = kWasmStmt
; break; } \
3857 case kExpr##Name: { \
3858 memtype = MachineType::Type(); \
3859 ret_type = kWasmStmt; \
3860 break; /* to generic mem access code below */ \
3861 }
3862 ATOMIC_STORE_OP_LIST(CASE_ATOMIC_STORE_OP)case kExprI32AtomicStore: { memtype = MachineType::Uint32(); ret_type
= kWasmStmt; break; } case kExprI64AtomicStore: { memtype = MachineType
::Uint64(); ret_type = kWasmStmt; break; } case kExprI32AtomicStore8U
: { memtype = MachineType::Uint8(); ret_type = kWasmStmt; break
; } case kExprI32AtomicStore16U: { memtype = MachineType::Uint16
(); ret_type = kWasmStmt; break; } case kExprI64AtomicStore8U
: { memtype = MachineType::Uint8(); ret_type = kWasmStmt; break
; } case kExprI64AtomicStore16U: { memtype = MachineType::Uint16
(); ret_type = kWasmStmt; break; } case kExprI64AtomicStore32U
: { memtype = MachineType::Uint32(); ret_type = kWasmStmt; break
; }
3863#undef CASE_ATOMIC_OP
3864#define CASE_ATOMIC_OP(Name, Type) \
3865 case kExpr##Name: { \
3866 memtype = MachineType::Type(); \
3867 ret_type = GetReturnType(sig); \
3868 break; /* to generic mem access code below */ \
3869 }
3870 ATOMIC_OP_LIST(CASE_ATOMIC_OP)CASE_ATOMIC_OP(AtomicNotify, Uint32) CASE_ATOMIC_OP(I32AtomicWait
, Uint32) CASE_ATOMIC_OP(I64AtomicWait, Uint64) CASE_ATOMIC_OP
(I32AtomicLoad, Uint32) CASE_ATOMIC_OP(I64AtomicLoad, Uint64)
CASE_ATOMIC_OP(I32AtomicLoad8U, Uint8) CASE_ATOMIC_OP(I32AtomicLoad16U
, Uint16) CASE_ATOMIC_OP(I64AtomicLoad8U, Uint8) CASE_ATOMIC_OP
(I64AtomicLoad16U, Uint16) CASE_ATOMIC_OP(I64AtomicLoad32U, Uint32
) CASE_ATOMIC_OP(I32AtomicAdd, Uint32) CASE_ATOMIC_OP(I32AtomicAdd8U
, Uint8) CASE_ATOMIC_OP(I32AtomicAdd16U, Uint16) CASE_ATOMIC_OP
(I64AtomicAdd, Uint64) CASE_ATOMIC_OP(I64AtomicAdd8U, Uint8) CASE_ATOMIC_OP
(I64AtomicAdd16U, Uint16) CASE_ATOMIC_OP(I64AtomicAdd32U, Uint32
) CASE_ATOMIC_OP(I32AtomicSub, Uint32) CASE_ATOMIC_OP(I64AtomicSub
, Uint64) CASE_ATOMIC_OP(I32AtomicSub8U, Uint8) CASE_ATOMIC_OP
(I32AtomicSub16U, Uint16) CASE_ATOMIC_OP(I64AtomicSub8U, Uint8
) CASE_ATOMIC_OP(I64AtomicSub16U, Uint16) CASE_ATOMIC_OP(I64AtomicSub32U
, Uint32) CASE_ATOMIC_OP(I32AtomicAnd, Uint32) CASE_ATOMIC_OP
(I64AtomicAnd, Uint64) CASE_ATOMIC_OP(I32AtomicAnd8U, Uint8) CASE_ATOMIC_OP
(I32AtomicAnd16U, Uint16) CASE_ATOMIC_OP(I64AtomicAnd8U, Uint8
) CASE_ATOMIC_OP(I64AtomicAnd16U, Uint16) CASE_ATOMIC_OP(I64AtomicAnd32U
, Uint32) CASE_ATOMIC_OP(I32AtomicOr, Uint32) CASE_ATOMIC_OP(
I64AtomicOr, Uint64) CASE_ATOMIC_OP(I32AtomicOr8U, Uint8) CASE_ATOMIC_OP
(I32AtomicOr16U, Uint16) CASE_ATOMIC_OP(I64AtomicOr8U, Uint8)
CASE_ATOMIC_OP(I64AtomicOr16U, Uint16) CASE_ATOMIC_OP(I64AtomicOr32U
, Uint32) CASE_ATOMIC_OP(I32AtomicXor, Uint32) CASE_ATOMIC_OP
(I64AtomicXor, Uint64) CASE_ATOMIC_OP(I32AtomicXor8U, Uint8) CASE_ATOMIC_OP
(I32AtomicXor16U, Uint16) CASE_ATOMIC_OP(I64AtomicXor8U, Uint8
) CASE_ATOMIC_OP(I64AtomicXor16U, Uint16) CASE_ATOMIC_OP(I64AtomicXor32U
, Uint32) CASE_ATOMIC_OP(I32AtomicExchange, Uint32) CASE_ATOMIC_OP
(I64AtomicExchange, Uint64) CASE_ATOMIC_OP(I32AtomicExchange8U
, Uint8) CASE_ATOMIC_OP(I32AtomicExchange16U, Uint16) CASE_ATOMIC_OP
(I64AtomicExchange8U, Uint8) CASE_ATOMIC_OP(I64AtomicExchange16U
, Uint16) CASE_ATOMIC_OP(I64AtomicExchange32U, Uint32) CASE_ATOMIC_OP
(I32AtomicCompareExchange, Uint32) CASE_ATOMIC_OP(I64AtomicCompareExchange
, Uint64) CASE_ATOMIC_OP(I32AtomicCompareExchange8U, Uint8) CASE_ATOMIC_OP
(I32AtomicCompareExchange16U, Uint16) CASE_ATOMIC_OP(I64AtomicCompareExchange8U
, Uint8) CASE_ATOMIC_OP(I64AtomicCompareExchange16U, Uint16) CASE_ATOMIC_OP
(I64AtomicCompareExchange32U, Uint32)
3871#undef CASE_ATOMIC_OP
3872 case kExprAtomicFence: {
3873 byte zero = this->template read_u8<validate>(this->pc_ + 2, "zero");
3874 if (!VALIDATE(zero == 0)) {
3875 this->error(this->pc_ + 2, "invalid atomic operand");
3876 return 0;
3877 }
3878 CALL_INTERFACE_IF_REACHABLE(AtomicFence);
3879 return 3;
3880 }
3881 default:
3882 this->error("invalid atomic opcode");
3883 return 0;
3884 }
3885 if (!CheckHasMemoryForAtomics()) return 0;
3886 MemoryAccessImmediate<validate> imm(
3887 this, this->pc_ + 2, ElementSizeLog2Of(memtype.representation()));
3888 ArgVector args = PopArgs(sig);
3889 Value* result = ret_type == kWasmStmt ? nullptr : Push(GetReturnType(sig));
3890 CALL_INTERFACE_IF_REACHABLE(AtomicOp, opcode, VectorOf(args), imm, result);
3891 return 2 + imm.length;
3892 }
3893
3894 unsigned DecodeNumericOpcode(WasmOpcode opcode) {
3895 const FunctionSig* sig = WasmOpcodes::Signature(opcode);
3896 if (!VALIDATE(sig != nullptr)) {
3897 this->error("invalid numeric opcode");
3898 return 0;
3899 }
3900 switch (opcode) {
3901 case kExprI32SConvertSatF32:
3902 case kExprI32UConvertSatF32:
3903 case kExprI32SConvertSatF64:
3904 case kExprI32UConvertSatF64:
3905 case kExprI64SConvertSatF32:
3906 case kExprI64UConvertSatF32:
3907 case kExprI64SConvertSatF64:
3908 case kExprI64UConvertSatF64:
3909 return 1 + BuildSimpleOperator(opcode, sig);
3910 case kExprMemoryInit: {
3911 MemoryInitImmediate<validate> imm(this, this->pc_ + 2);
3912 if (!this->Validate(this->pc_ + 2, imm)) return 0;
3913 Value size = Pop(2, sig->GetParam(2));
3914 Value src = Pop(1, sig->GetParam(1));
3915 Value dst = Pop(0, sig->GetParam(0));
3916 CALL_INTERFACE_IF_REACHABLE(MemoryInit, imm, dst, src, size);
3917 return 2 + imm.length;
3918 }
3919 case kExprDataDrop: {
3920 DataDropImmediate<validate> imm(this, this->pc_ + 2);
3921 if (!this->Validate(this->pc_ + 2, imm)) return 0;
3922 CALL_INTERFACE_IF_REACHABLE(DataDrop, imm);
3923 return 2 + imm.length;
3924 }
3925 case kExprMemoryCopy: {
3926 MemoryCopyImmediate<validate> imm(this, this->pc_ + 2);
3927 if (!this->Validate(this->pc_ + 2, imm)) return 0;
3928 Value size = Pop(2, sig->GetParam(2));
3929 Value src = Pop(1, sig->GetParam(1));
3930 Value dst = Pop(0, sig->GetParam(0));
3931 CALL_INTERFACE_IF_REACHABLE(MemoryCopy, imm, dst, src, size);
3932 return 2 + imm.length;
3933 }
3934 case kExprMemoryFill: {
3935 MemoryIndexImmediate<validate> imm(this, this->pc_ + 2);
3936 if (!this->Validate(this->pc_ + 2, imm)) return 0;
3937 Value size = Pop(2, sig->GetParam(2));
3938 Value value = Pop(1, sig->GetParam(1));
3939 Value dst = Pop(0, sig->GetParam(0));
3940 CALL_INTERFACE_IF_REACHABLE(MemoryFill, imm, dst, value, size);
3941 return 2 + imm.length;
3942 }
3943 case kExprTableInit: {
3944 TableInitImmediate<validate> imm(this, this->pc_ + 2);
3945 if (!this->Validate(this->pc_ + 2, imm)) return 0;
3946 ArgVector args = PopArgs(sig);
3947 CALL_INTERFACE_IF_REACHABLE(TableInit, imm, VectorOf(args));
3948 return 2 + imm.length;
3949 }
3950 case kExprElemDrop: {
3951 ElemDropImmediate<validate> imm(this, this->pc_ + 2);
3952 if (!this->Validate(this->pc_ + 2, imm)) return 0;
3953 CALL_INTERFACE_IF_REACHABLE(ElemDrop, imm);
3954 return 2 + imm.length;
3955 }
3956 case kExprTableCopy: {
3957 TableCopyImmediate<validate> imm(this, this->pc_ + 2);
3958 if (!this->Validate(this->pc_ + 2, imm)) return 0;
3959 ArgVector args = PopArgs(sig);
3960 CALL_INTERFACE_IF_REACHABLE(TableCopy, imm, VectorOf(args));
3961 return 2 + imm.length;
3962 }
3963 case kExprTableGrow: {
3964 TableIndexImmediate<validate> imm(this, this->pc_ + 2);
3965 if (!this->Validate(this->pc_ + 2, imm)) return 0;
3966 Value delta = Pop(1, sig->GetParam(1));
3967 Value value = Pop(0, this->module_->tables[imm.index].type);
3968 Value* result = Push(kWasmI32);
3969 CALL_INTERFACE_IF_REACHABLE(TableGrow, imm, value, delta, result);
3970 return 2 + imm.length;
3971 }
3972 case kExprTableSize: {
3973 TableIndexImmediate<validate> imm(this, this->pc_ + 2);
3974 if (!this->Validate(this->pc_ + 2, imm)) return 0;
3975 Value* result = Push(kWasmI32);
3976 CALL_INTERFACE_IF_REACHABLE(TableSize, imm, result);
3977 return 2 + imm.length;
3978 }
3979 case kExprTableFill: {
3980 TableIndexImmediate<validate> imm(this, this->pc_ + 2);
3981 if (!this->Validate(this->pc_ + 2, imm)) return 0;
3982 Value count = Pop(2, sig->GetParam(2));
3983 Value value = Pop(1, this->module_->tables[imm.index].type);
3984 Value start = Pop(0, sig->GetParam(0));
3985 CALL_INTERFACE_IF_REACHABLE(TableFill, imm, start, value, count);
3986 return 2 + imm.length;
3987 }
3988 default:
3989 this->error("invalid numeric opcode");
3990 return 0;
3991 }
3992 }
3993
3994 void DoReturn() {
3995 size_t return_count = this->sig_->return_count();
3996 if (return_count > 1) {
3997 this->detected_->Add(kFeature_mv);
3998 }
3999 DCHECK_GE(stack_.size(), return_count)((void) 0);
4000 Vector<Value> return_values =
4001 return_count == 0
4002 ? Vector<Value>{}
4003 : Vector<Value>{&*(stack_.end() - return_count), return_count};
4004
4005 CALL_INTERFACE_IF_REACHABLE(DoReturn, return_values);
4006 }
4007
4008 V8_INLINEinline __attribute__((always_inline)) Value* Push(ValueType type) {
4009 DCHECK_NE(kWasmStmt, type)((void) 0);
4010 stack_.emplace_back(this->pc_, type);
4011 return &stack_.back();
4012 }
4013
4014 void PushMergeValues(Control* c, Merge<Value>* merge) {
4015 DCHECK_EQ(c, &control_.back())((void) 0);
4016 DCHECK(merge == &c->start_merge || merge == &c->end_merge)((void) 0);
4017 stack_.erase(stack_.begin() + c->stack_depth, stack_.end());
4018 if (merge->arity == 1) {
4019 stack_.push_back(merge->vals.first);
4020 } else {
4021 for (uint32_t i = 0; i < merge->arity; i++) {
4022 stack_.push_back(merge->vals.array[i]);
4023 }
4024 }
4025 DCHECK_EQ(c->stack_depth + merge->arity, stack_.size())((void) 0);
4026 }
4027
4028 Value* PushReturns(const FunctionSig* sig) {
4029 size_t return_count = sig->return_count();
4030 if (return_count == 0) return nullptr;
4031 size_t old_size = stack_.size();
4032 for (size_t i = 0; i < return_count; ++i) {
4033 Push(sig->GetReturn(i));
4034 }
4035 return stack_.data() + old_size;
4036 }
4037
4038 // We do not inline these functions because doing so causes a large binary
4039 // size increase. Not inlining them should not create a performance
4040 // degradation, because their invocations are guarded by V8_LIKELY.
4041 V8_NOINLINE__attribute__((noinline)) void PopTypeError(int index, Value val, ValueType expected) {
4042 this->errorf(val.pc, "%s[%d] expected type %s, found %s of type %s",
4043 SafeOpcodeNameAt(this->pc_), index, expected.name().c_str(),
4044 SafeOpcodeNameAt(val.pc), val.type.name().c_str());
4045 }
4046
4047 V8_NOINLINE__attribute__((noinline)) void NotEnoughArgumentsError(int index) {
4048 this->errorf(this->pc_,
4049 "not enough arguments on the stack for %s, expected %d more",
4050 SafeOpcodeNameAt(this->pc_), index + 1);
4051 }
4052
4053 V8_INLINEinline __attribute__((always_inline)) Value Pop(int index, ValueType expected) {
4054 Value val = Pop(index);
4055 if (!VALIDATE(IsSubtypeOf(val.type, expected, this->module_) ||
4056 val.type == kWasmBottom || expected == kWasmBottom)) {
4057 PopTypeError(index, val, expected);
4058 }
4059 return val;
4060 }
4061
4062 V8_INLINEinline __attribute__((always_inline)) Value Pop(int index) {
4063 DCHECK(!control_.empty())((void) 0);
4064 uint32_t limit = control_.back().stack_depth;
4065 if (stack_.size() <= limit) {
4066 // Popping past the current control start in reachable code.
4067 if (!VALIDATE(control_.back().unreachable())) {
4068 NotEnoughArgumentsError(index);
4069 }
4070 return UnreachableValue(this->pc_);
4071 }
4072 Value val = stack_.back();
4073 stack_.pop_back();
4074 return val;
4075 }
4076
4077 // Pops values from the stack, as defined by {merge}. Thereby we type-check
4078 // unreachable merges. Afterwards the values are pushed again on the stack
4079 // according to the signature in {merge}. This is done so follow-up validation
4080 // is possible.
4081 bool TypeCheckUnreachableMerge(Merge<Value>& merge, bool conditional_branch) {
4082 int arity = merge.arity;
4083 // For conditional branches, stack value '0' is the condition of the branch,
4084 // and the result values start at index '1'.
4085 int index_offset = conditional_branch ? 1 : 0;
4086 for (int i = arity - 1; i >= 0; --i) Pop(index_offset + i, merge[i].type);
4087 // Push values of the correct type back on the stack.
4088 for (int i = 0; i < arity; ++i) Push(merge[i].type);
4089 return this->ok();
4090 }
4091
4092 int startrel(const byte* ptr) { return static_cast<int>(ptr - this->start_); }
4093
4094 void FallThruTo(Control* c) {
4095 DCHECK_EQ(c, &control_.back())((void) 0);
4096 if (!TypeCheckFallThru()) return;
4097 if (!c->reachable()) return;
4098
4099 if (!c->is_loop()) CALL_INTERFACE(FallThruTo, c);
4100 c->end_merge.reached = true;
4101 }
4102
4103 bool TypeCheckMergeValues(Control* c, Merge<Value>* merge) {
4104 // This is a CHECK instead of a DCHECK because {validate} is a constexpr,
4105 // and a CHECK makes the whole function unreachable.
4106 static_assert(validate, "Call this function only within VALIDATE");
4107 DCHECK(merge == &c->start_merge || merge == &c->end_merge)((void) 0);
4108 DCHECK_GE(stack_.size(), c->stack_depth + merge->arity)((void) 0);
4109 // The computation of {stack_values} is only valid if {merge->arity} is >0.
4110 DCHECK_LT(0, merge->arity)((void) 0);
4111 Value* stack_values = &*(stack_.end() - merge->arity);
4112 // Typecheck the topmost {merge->arity} values on the stack.
4113 for (uint32_t i = 0; i < merge->arity; ++i) {
4114 Value& val = stack_values[i];
4115 Value& old = (*merge)[i];
4116 if (!VALIDATE(IsSubtypeOf(val.type, old.type, this->module_))) {
4117 this->errorf(this->pc_, "type error in merge[%u] (expected %s, got %s)",
4118 i, old.type.name().c_str(), val.type.name().c_str());
4119 return false;
4120 }
4121 }
4122
4123 return true;
4124 }
4125
4126 bool TypeCheckOneArmedIf(Control* c) {
4127 static_assert(validate, "Call this function only within VALIDATE");
4128 DCHECK(c->is_onearmed_if())((void) 0);
4129 DCHECK_EQ(c->start_merge.arity, c->end_merge.arity)((void) 0);
4130 for (uint32_t i = 0; i < c->start_merge.arity; ++i) {
4131 Value& start = c->start_merge[i];
4132 Value& end = c->end_merge[i];
4133 if (!VALIDATE(IsSubtypeOf(start.type, end.type, this->module_))) {
4134 this->errorf(this->pc_, "type error in merge[%u] (expected %s, got %s)",
4135 i, end.type.name().c_str(), start.type.name().c_str());
4136 return false;
4137 }
4138 }
4139
4140 return true;
4141 }
4142
4143 bool TypeCheckFallThru() {
4144 static_assert(validate, "Call this function only within VALIDATE");
4145 Control& c = control_.back();
4146 if (V8_LIKELY(c.reachable())(__builtin_expect(!!(c.reachable()), 1))) {
4147 uint32_t expected = c.end_merge.arity;
4148 DCHECK_GE(stack_.size(), c.stack_depth)((void) 0);
4149 uint32_t actual = static_cast<uint32_t>(stack_.size()) - c.stack_depth;
4150 // Fallthrus must match the arity of the control exactly.
4151 if (!VALIDATE(actual == expected)) {
4152 this->errorf(
4153 this->pc_,
4154 "expected %u elements on the stack for fallthru to @%d, found %u",
4155 expected, startrel(c.pc), actual);
4156 return false;
4157 }
4158 if (expected == 0) return true; // Fast path.
4159
4160 return TypeCheckMergeValues(&c, &c.end_merge);
4161 }
4162
4163 // Type-check an unreachable fallthru. First we do an arity check, then a
4164 // type check. Note that type-checking may require an adjustment of the
4165 // stack, if some stack values are missing to match the block signature.
4166 Merge<Value>& merge = c.end_merge;
4167 int arity = static_cast<int>(merge.arity);
4168 int available = static_cast<int>(stack_.size()) - c.stack_depth;
4169 // For fallthrus, not more than the needed values should be available.
4170 if (!VALIDATE(available <= arity)) {
4171 this->errorf(
4172 this->pc_,
4173 "expected %u elements on the stack for fallthru to @%d, found %u",
4174 arity, startrel(c.pc), available);
4175 return false;
4176 }
4177 // Pop all values from the stack for type checking of existing stack
4178 // values.
4179 return TypeCheckUnreachableMerge(merge, false);
4180 }
4181
4182 enum TypeCheckBranchResult {
4183 kReachableBranch,
4184 kUnreachableBranch,
4185 kInvalidStack,
4186 };
4187
4188 TypeCheckBranchResult TypeCheckBranch(Control* c, bool conditional_branch) {
4189 if (V8_LIKELY(control_.back().reachable())(__builtin_expect(!!(control_.back().reachable()), 1))) {
4190 // We only do type-checking here. This is only needed during validation.
4191 if (!validate) return kReachableBranch;
4192
4193 // Branches must have at least the number of values expected; can have
4194 // more.
4195 uint32_t expected = c->br_merge()->arity;
4196 if (expected == 0) return kReachableBranch; // Fast path.
4197 DCHECK_GE(stack_.size(), control_.back().stack_depth)((void) 0);
4198 uint32_t actual =
4199 static_cast<uint32_t>(stack_.size()) - control_.back().stack_depth;
4200 if (!VALIDATE(actual >= expected)) {
4201 this->errorf(
4202 this->pc_,
4203 "expected %u elements on the stack for br to @%d, found %u",
4204 expected, startrel(c->pc), actual);
4205 return kInvalidStack;
4206 }
4207 return TypeCheckMergeValues(c, c->br_merge()) ? kReachableBranch
4208 : kInvalidStack;
4209 }
4210
4211 return TypeCheckUnreachableMerge(*c->br_merge(), conditional_branch)
4212 ? kUnreachableBranch
4213 : kInvalidStack;
4214 }
4215
4216 bool TypeCheckReturn() {
4217 int num_returns = static_cast<int>(this->sig_->return_count());
4218 // No type checking is needed if there are no returns.
4219 if (num_returns == 0) return true;
4220
4221 // Returns must have at least the number of values expected; can have more.
4222 int num_available =
4223 static_cast<int>(stack_.size()) - control_.back().stack_depth;
4224 if (!VALIDATE(num_available >= num_returns)) {
4225 this->errorf(this->pc_,
4226 "expected %u elements on the stack for return, found %u",
4227 num_returns, num_available);
4228 return false;
4229 }
4230
4231 // Typecheck the topmost {num_returns} values on the stack.
4232 // This line requires num_returns > 0.
4233 Value* stack_values = &*(stack_.end() - num_returns);
4234 for (int i = 0; i < num_returns; ++i) {
4235 Value& val = stack_values[i];
4236 ValueType expected_type = this->sig_->GetReturn(i);
4237 if (!VALIDATE(IsSubtypeOf(val.type, expected_type, this->module_))) {
4238 this->errorf(this->pc_,
4239 "type error in return[%u] (expected %s, got %s)", i,
4240 expected_type.name().c_str(), val.type.name().c_str());
4241 return false;
4242 }
4243 }
4244 return true;
4245 }
4246
4247 void onFirstError() override {
4248 this->end_ = this->pc_; // Terminate decoding loop.
4249 this->current_code_reachable_ = false;
4250 TRACE(" !%s\n", this->error_.message().c_str());
4251 CALL_INTERFACE(OnFirstError);
4252 }
4253
4254 int BuildSimplePrototypeOperator(WasmOpcode opcode) {
4255 if (opcode == kExprRefEq) {
4256 CHECK_PROTOTYPE_OPCODE(gc);
4257 }
4258 const FunctionSig* sig = WasmOpcodes::Signature(opcode);
4259 return BuildSimpleOperator(opcode, sig);
4260 }
4261
4262 int BuildSimpleOperator(WasmOpcode opcode, const FunctionSig* sig) {
4263 DCHECK_GE(1, sig->return_count())((void) 0);
4264 ValueType ret = sig->return_count() == 0 ? kWasmStmt : sig->GetReturn(0);
4265 if (sig->parameter_count() == 1) {
4266 return BuildSimpleOperator(opcode, ret, sig->GetParam(0));
4267 } else {
4268 DCHECK_EQ(2, sig->parameter_count())((void) 0);
4269 return BuildSimpleOperator(opcode, ret, sig->GetParam(0),
4270 sig->GetParam(1));
4271 }
4272 }
4273
4274 int BuildSimpleOperator(WasmOpcode opcode, ValueType return_type,
4275 ValueType arg_type) {
4276 Value val = Pop(0, arg_type);
4277 Value* ret = return_type == kWasmStmt ? nullptr : Push(return_type);
4278 CALL_INTERFACE_IF_REACHABLE(UnOp, opcode, val, ret);
4279 return 1;
4280 }
4281
4282 int BuildSimpleOperator(WasmOpcode opcode, ValueType return_type,
4283 ValueType lhs_type, ValueType rhs_type) {
4284 Value rval = Pop(1, rhs_type);
4285 Value lval = Pop(0, lhs_type);
4286 Value* ret = return_type == kWasmStmt ? nullptr : Push(return_type);
4287 CALL_INTERFACE_IF_REACHABLE(BinOp, opcode, lval, rval, ret);
4288 return 1;
4289 }
4290
4291#define DEFINE_SIMPLE_SIG_OPERATOR(sig, ...) \
4292 int BuildSimpleOperator_##sig(WasmOpcode opcode) { \
4293 return BuildSimpleOperator(opcode, __VA_ARGS__); \
4294 }
